Japan's Countermeasures for Next Year's Naval Disarmament Conference 27

Determining Four Fundamental Principles

Designating the Philippine Islands as a Buffer Zone

Opinions from the Navy Ministry Are Gradually Rising

(Tokyo) With the World Disarmament Conference approaching next year, Japan's fundamental principles in this regard are roughly based on the following four items to create a specific proposal: (1) Ensure national defense security; (2) Maintain the right to equal armament; (3) Eliminate the doctrine of naval category and proportional restrictions; (4) Limit armament due to the free construction of ships under the doctrine of total tonnage, that is, Japan always stands on the fundamental principle of mutual non-aggression. If legitimate demands are not recognized and the conference breaks down, the responsibility should be borne by the United Kingdom and the United States. Recently, within the Navy Ministry, the following informal opinions have gradually risen, causing attention from all parties: regarding the independence of the Philippine Islands, based on the absolute trust between the United States and Japan, guarantee the independence and neutrality of the Philippine Islands, with the island as a non-defensive buffer zone. In addition, Qam Island is the same as Japan's mandated rule in the South Pacific. Cancel the restriction of the Western Pacific defense agreement and restore the free defense state before the conclusion of the Washington Treaty. Then the United States will completely entrust the maintenance of peace in the Far East to Japan, enjoy the benefits of the open door and equal opportunity in the Orient, and establish a policy agreement such as this to sweep away the suspicions between the two countries. The two countries will restore a true friendly relationship. At that time, because the Philippine Islands are a buffer zone, the anxiety of the United Kingdom's Australia and other Pacific coastal territories can be eliminated. At the 1935 disarmament conference, naval armament issues can be easily resolved according to the above four fundamental principles of Japan. (Dian Tong News on the 4th)

Japanese Army Minister Follows Existing Rules and Promotes Improving National Defense 28

(Tokyo) In view of Japan's special circumstances after the Manchurian Incident and the internal situation, Army Minister Hayashi believes that it is necessary to improve national defense in terms of politics, economy, and diplomacy. After the parliament is completed, he will promote improvement at an appropriate time. Army Minister Hayashi is currently studying and implementing the principles and policies left by former Army Minister Araki, generally according to the following principles: (1) The improvement method must be drafted under the current institution; (2) The scope of improvement, although it involves all matters that hinder national defense, is limited to matters that are purely related to national defense. (Dian Tong News on the 4th)

The Political Situation in Japan Remains Chaotic After Hatoyama Resigns 29

Various Factions Observe That the Current Cabinet Will Inevitably Collapse Sooner or Later

After the Closing of Parliament, Saito Will Visit Prince Saionji to Determine His Course of Action

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Saito will wait until the current parliament is completed, restore the party situation with the Seiyukai, and then replenish cabinet members to remain in the cabinet. However, during this parliament, due to the replacement of two core cabinet members, the public is quite dissatisfied with the current cabinet's policies and measures. Therefore, after the completion of this parliament, due to the political situation, it is also believed that some people will resign. But all the mysteries are in the mind of Elder Prince Saionji. Therefore, after the completion of parliament, Prime Minister Saito will visit Prince Saionji to decide his course of action. (Dian Tong News on the 4th)

(Tokyo) The political developments after the resignation of Minister of Education Hatoyama are now being watched by all parties. The observations of various political parties also differ depending on their positions and are completely in a chaotic state. The observations of various political parties are recorded separately as follows:

"Seiyukai" has two opposing observations: (1) The current cabinet continues to have problems with discipline. Ministers Nakajima and Hatoyama have resigned one after another. Regardless of the reasons for their resignation, Prime Minister Saito's responsibility for reporting to the Emperor is inevitable. Moreover, the opinions of Ministers Goto and Nagai differ on the issue of rice control within the cabinet, exposing the disunity of the cabinet. Moreover, those who should oppose the current cabinet have generally disappeared, so there is no expectation and it cannot continue. Although it may pass through parliament, it will inevitably collapse. As for the replenishment of Minister of Education Hatoyama, since there is no negotiation with the Seiyukai and no indication of any kind, it is to understand the situation in between. (2) It is said that the reason for not replenishing Minister of Education Hatoyama's re-appointment is that if the budget is approved, the parliament will replenish it again. This is a cunning method of Prime Minister Saito's faction to alleviate the opposition air of the House of Peers. After the completion of the parliament, they will seek a strategy to stay in the cabinet for a long time. Therefore, either under the pretext that a successor has not been obtained, or that Prince Saionji does not want a political change, they will replenish the Minister of Education alone, or implement a partial reorganization of the cabinet to seek a long-term stay. As for the Seiyukai itself, because of the current political situation, even if a political change occurs, the party has no hope of political power, so it will temporarily maintain the status quo and wait until the atmosphere of restoring the party cabinet is brewing before hoping to resign en masse.

"Minseito" Now that Minister of Education Hatoyama has resigned, the budget and the rural relief budget should be passed safely. Also, the issue of control of foreign rice has also been in accordance with the hopes of the House of Representatives and should be decided soon. The result may be to pass through parliament, but after the completion of parliament, due to the difficulty of replenishing the Minister of Education, it is said that there will be a general resignation, but Ministers Takahashi and Yamamoto both agree to maintain the cabinet, so the result is always a smooth solution, and the budget for the fiscal year of Showa 10 will also be prepared.

"National Alliance" The current cabinet does not show any reflection on our party's motion of no confidence. This parliament may be able to pass safely, but it has completely exposed the incompetence of the current cabinet. Therefore, after the parliament, the prime minister will visit Saionji to express his intention to resign. As for the successor cabinet, it is not a party cabinet, which can be asserted. This parliament is an excellent opportunity for political parties to restore credibility, but they have lost credibility due to the problem of discipline. As for the successor cabinet, it must be a powerful cabinet that can open up the national policy in extraordinary times and can implement it. Therefore, the Hiranuma cabinet is more suitable.

"House of Peers" Since both Ministers Nakajima and Hatoyama have resigned from the current cabinet, the House of Peers does not want to take the responsibility for overthrowing the current cabinet and will not actively attack the current government. However, the current cabinet has no means to open up extraordinary times, so at this time, the House of Peers should have an expression of intent. As for the re-appointment of the Minister of Education, the person recommended by Seiyukai President Suzuki does not meet the government's expectations, and the Seiyukai does not want to hear what the government wants. If it is sought outside the political parties, it will break away from the Seiyukai, and a political crisis will occur. If so, then the current cabinet is about to reach the handover period. (Dian Tong News on the 4th)

British-Japanese Trade Negotiations Are on the Verge of Collapse 30

Japanese Representatives Will Propose a Recess

To Avoid Responsibility for Rupture

Osaka Regarding the Joint Committee on Countermeasures for British-Japanese Trade Negotiations, opinions have already been unified regarding the timing of the withdrawal of cotton industry representatives, namely: (1) In order to avoid the rupture of the negotiations, after observing the progress of the fourth meeting on the 7th, instruct the delegation to propose a recess to the United Kingdom and immediately carry out the withdrawal; (2) Until that time, firmly advocate the established policy and never concede. Also, after the committee adjourned yesterday, Chairman Kawabe issued a statement in the form of a speech as follows: (1) It is regrettable that the United Kingdom proposed an agreement on third-country markets that could not be implemented at the beginning of the meeting, putting the negotiations on the verge of collapse; (2) If the world market is to be the scope of the agreement, a world cotton industry conference should be held to agree on the production and export of cotton products. It is illegal to restrict exports only to Japan; (3) Japan is also negotiating with the Netherlands, Turkey, Egypt, Africa, etc., so an agreement on third-country markets is impossible; (4) It is heard that if Japan does not agree to the third-country market agreement, the British government will completely prevent Japanese cotton cloth and rayon from being imported to threaten Japan. If the negotiations break down, it will further stand on a common front with European countries to prevent Japanese goods. If this is the case, it is regrettable for international trade and British-Japanese relations. (Dian Tong News on the 4th)

Has Obtained Understanding from the US Side

Everything that our country needs is the principle of purchase and transportation. It is rumored that the US authorities fully understand our country's request, but there is still a difference in the amount of reduction. New Policies After the American Blue Eagle Movement (New York Correspondence) 87

Reducing Currency Value to Develop Foreign Trade

Recovering Overseas Loans to Overcome Economic Panic

Since the implementation of the Blue Eagle Movement, the American economy seems to have improved, and people generally express their happiness. However, in fact, the goods manufactured by factories are still stacked in warehouses, and only a small minority is consumed by consumers. Moreover, most people are still poor, and the extent of their poverty has not diminished compared to before the implementation of the National Industrial Recovery Act. Therefore, most Americans, who used to live in New York and only knew how to blindly enjoy themselves and follow fashion, now only know how to complain. They have given up their private cars and are riding rental cars. Those who cannot afford rental cars are riding public buses. The enjoyment of life has decreased, but few people are still investigating the causes of the economic panic. Political interest is still very cold. British foreign policy, French strategies, Japanese aggressive invasion, and German fierce pursuit all seem irrelevant to American society. They do not pay close attention to these political and economic situations with enthusiasm. Everything abroad absolutely cannot outweigh their enthusiasm for trade and accumulating money. Even the restoration of diplomatic relations with the Soviet Union is more of a calculation for expanding trade than a political implication.

Unfortunately, there is no longer a golden age like the early days of the European War for the United States to fully develop. The markets of overseas countries are occupied by strong competitors, and consumers are very weak. They do not have much spare capacity to enjoy American expensive products. European consumers have relatively greater purchasing power, but each country is closing its doors to be self-sufficient. Therefore, the implementation of the Blue Eagle Movement, shortening working hours, increasing wages, and reducing capitalists' profits, is a new transformation of capital organization and a new method in 1933. However, the effect is still very small and cannot be considered a solution to the urgent situation in the United States. If this continues, not only will it be impossible to overcome the panic, but even temporary stability cannot be achieved.

Therefore, new tricks are being tried again. This is the method of reducing the pure gold content of the American dollar, which was announced on January 31. According to this method, the new gold dollar is 15 grams cold and twenty-one and five points (the old US dollar is 25.8 grams cold), which is 59.06 percent of the old currency. The reduced component is about 41 percent. Due to the decrease in currency value, the government can obtain a profit of 2.686 billion US dollars, but 2 billion US dollars will be drawn from it as a fund to stabilize the currency. The reasons why the American president wants to adopt an inflationary policy are approximately the following four points:

(1) The turnover in the financial sector is also gradually becoming less flexible. There are few industrial investments, so interest rates naturally decrease. The public works projects undertaken by the government are very limited in terms of production significance, so monetary inflation policy must be used to support finance and increase its monopoly power, while stimulating emerging industries.

(2) The US dollar has indeed fallen in international exchange rates, but it is not stable, so the export of goods has not seen a rapid increase. American products overseas still cannot compete with Japan and Britain. This is why the currency value is simply reduced to seek an increase in the price of goods, while seeking benefits from exporting abroad.

(3) Most of the United States' foreign investments are frozen and difficult to recover. Although there is more than one reason for the freeze, the excessively high exchange rate of the US dollar is one of the important reasons. In the future, if the value of the US dollar is reduced, the recovery of investment will be easier. At the same time, debtors at home will also get a little benefit. If most people can repay their debts, the circulation of finance will be more prosperous.

(4) The US government will issue 600 billion US dollars of government bonds before June of this year. In the current situation, the American people may not have the ability to consume them, and the unstable currency value also prevents people from investing lightly. The current method can stabilize the currency price, and people will be happy to invest, so there is hope for the government's financial resources.

This is the hope of the Roosevelt government, and also the hope of the general American public, hoping to gradually restore the past prosperity from this. But in reality, will it be like the Blue Eagle Movement? It is still a question. It is not easy to truly get a solution. (February 1, 1934)

Japanese Army in Tianjin Conducts Demonstration Exercise 88

The Exercise Location Is Actually in the Hinterland of Hebei

The General Affairs Office of the Jinpu Railway Arbitrarily Allocates Cars

Tianjin Correspondence, Today (the 1st) is the date of Puyi's usurpation in Guanwai. The Japanese army stationed in Tianjin specially held a large-scale exercise. At 4:00 AM, the Japanese army, led by Commander of the Garrison Army Nakamura Koutaro, took a train to Jinghai County on the Tianjin-Pukou Railway line south of Tianjin. At 8:00 AM, they began field exercises. It is said that this exercise by the Japanese army has actually exceeded the scope of previous exercises. Its meaning is probably to take advantage of Puyi's usurpation to demonstrate to the people of North China. A week ago, the Commander of the Japanese Garrison Army sent a letter to the Hebei Provincial Government regarding the location of the exercise, stating that on March 1, he would conduct field exercises in Liangwangzhuang, Duliuhe, and Tangguantun on the Tianjin-Pukou Railway line in Jinghai County, south of Tianjin, and requested our side to allow it and inform the people. On the one hand, he sent personnel to the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Bureau to request the allocation of cars. Shi Yuxiao, who was in Ping, instructed the foreign affairs secretary of the provincial government to reply to the Japanese side by telephone, telling them that Jinghai belongs to the interior of Hebei and foreign troops cannot be allowed to conduct exercises there. After receiving the reply, the Japanese army sent another letter, raising three points: (1) A few years ago, the Chinese government allowed American troops to conduct an exercise in the area, which means that the area has a precedent for allowing foreign troops to conduct exercises. Based on this point, Japanese troops must also be allowed to conduct exercises. (2) A few years ago, the Japanese army conducted exercises in Daxing County, Hebei. Daxing and Jinghai both belong to Hebei counties. Since exercises were allowed in Daxing, they should also be allowed in Jinghai. (3) Last year, the Hebei Provincial Government allowed the Japanese army to conduct exercises in Nankou. What is the difference between Jinghai and Nankou? Moreover, they are both on the railway line, and Jinghai should not be declared as the hinterland. The wording of the letter was firm, indicating that there was no possibility of granting the request. Shi Yuxiao then forwarded the request to the Military Branch Political Committee in Ping for review. However, both committees have not yet responded. The Japanese side directly contacted Gao Hengru, the Chief of the General Affairs Office of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway, to negotiate the allocation of cars. Gao actually did not ask his superiors and privately agreed, and allocated a train of cars, parked at Tianjin East Station for the Japanese army to use. Secretly, he instructed the Japanese to negotiate with the Hebei Provincial Government. If they obtained an order from the provincial government, he would immediately drive the train. The Japanese army headquarters then sent personnel to visit Shi Yuxiao. Since Shi Yuxiao was in Ping and had not returned, they urgently urged the responsible person of the provincial government to reply. Shi Yuxiao, upon hearing the news in Ping, returned to Tianjin on the evening of February 28. The Japanese side then sent personnel to meet Shi Yuxiao, demanding an order to drive the train. Shi Yuxiao said that traffic matters are the responsibility of the traffic authorities, so how could the provincial government be forced to issue an order? He then summoned Gao Hengru to inquire. At this point, Gao stated the truth, saying that he had received a telegram from the General Bureau a few days ago, prohibiting him from allocating cars for the Japanese army. The car affairs office, upon receiving the order, disbanded the train that had been allocated. However, because the Japanese were pestering him, he could not refuse, so he had agreed, but he did not dare to act arbitrarily, fearing responsibility, so he pushed it to the provincial government. Shi Yuxiao then became displeased. However, because Gao had already privately promised, he could not go back on his word. In order to maintain national rights and the prestige of the province, he showed the telegram from the Tianjin-Pukou Railway General Bureau to the Japanese side, telling them that the authority did not belong to the provincial government and they could negotiate with the Railway Bureau. At this point, the Japanese side knew that it was not the responsibility of the provincial government and turned to pressure Gao Hengru again. Gao could not withstand the intimidation of the Japanese and, in his private capacity, coordinated with the Beining Railway Bureau for a train of cars. Today (the 1st), a special train was opened to Jinghai, carrying the Japanese army. It is estimated that about 300 Japanese soldiers went by train, and the majority marched on foot. The exercise will last for four days. The participating troops include about 300 infantry, cavalry, and artillery, as well as three tanks and six armored vehicles, divided into attacking and defending teams, conducting large-scale exercises along the Tianjin-Pukou Railway. It is hoped that the authorities are clearly aware that the Japanese army is demonstrating. Because the Tianjin-Pukou Railway arbitrarily allocated cars, the Japanese army was able to travel without permission. It is feared that once this precedent is set, the Japanese army may request to conduct marches and exercises in our inland areas at any time in the future. Therefore, it is proposed to telegraph the Ministry of Railways to investigate Gao Hengru for allocating cars. (March 1)

Mutual Killing of Minnan Quanzhou-Yongchun Militias 89

Hong Wende Occupies Yongchun

Zhang Xiongnan Defends Dehua

Both Sides Aiming for Territory

Xiamen Correspondence, With the end of military affairs in Fujian Province, the complex militia problem is the biggest issue. Recently, the old troops of Chen Guohui, the largest force in the Quanzhou area, led by Hong Wende, and the Dehua militia of Zhang Xiongnan are killing each other in Anxi. Zhang's troops are stationed in Yongchun, and Hong's troops are stationed in Nan'an. The war was launched on February 26. Hong's troops attacked Zhang in three routes: the central route led by Peng Tang, the western route led by Chen Yucai. Peng Tang's Nan'an First Detachment, Peng Deshan, departed from Jintao and joined Li Zhong, Zheng Mingzhi, etc. in Shishan to form the central route, directly attacking Yongchun via the Quanzhou-Yongchun-Dehua highway. Chen Yucai dispatched the recently incorporated remnants of the 19th Route Army, Shi Baoqi's unit, from Anxi to attack Dapu, to intercept Zhang's retreat from Penghu via Sukeng to Dehua. Hong also transferred Liu Chaoran's unit from Jinbei to the eastern route, attacking the eastern gate of Yongchun via Badu, leaving three or four squads in the Lijiuzhi area to block Zhang's retreat to Dehua. On the morning of the 26th, the central route, Peng Tang, arrived near Nanwushi, at the border of Nan'an and Yongchun, and made contact with the vanguard of Zhang's troops. The two sides engaged in a fierce battle. Zhang's troops were unable to resist and retreated to Xiaohu at noon. Peng's troops continued to advance and engaged in battle again in Xiaohu for several hours. Zhang's troops originally only had one company stationed in Xiaohu and then added two more companies, but they were still outnumbered and retreated again to Yongchun County. Peng took advantage of the victory to pursue and seized Niutouzhai. The vanguard advanced to the airfield outside the county seat. Zhang urgently transferred a large force to meet the enemy. Peng's troops, fearing encirclement due to the failure of the left and right wings to arrive at the same time, retreated out of Yongchun and back to Niutouzhai, where they were ambushed by Zhang's troops. Zheng Yonglai, the battalion commander of Peng's troops, was killed in action. They retreated to Wupushan in Nan'an. Zhang's troops pursued and engaged in a fierce battle at Changtan Bridge, on the border of Nan'an and Yongchun. Both sides suffered heavy casualties. The battle ended late in the evening. On the morning of the 27th, Peng Tang again dispatched a large force on more than ten trucks and counterattacked Yongchun. Hong Wende also transferred Liu Chaoran's troops to Shishan that day. Liu personally led the Tianying and Liu's directly subordinate units, a total of more than 500 people, departing from Heshi and Shishan, joining Peng Tang's 800-plus troops, with Liu's Tianying as the vanguard, to counterattack Yongchun. Zhang Xiongnan's troops, defending Changtan Bridge, Nanwushi, and Xiaohu, were unable to resist and retreated while fighting. By about 4:00 PM, Zhang's troops had retreated to Huangtianyang, and Peng's troops occupied Xiaohu, confronting Zhang's troops. At the same time, Hong's western route, Chen Yucai, with Shi Baoqi's regiment as the vanguard, advanced to Dapu in Yongchun and also made contact with Zhang Xiongnan's troops, then occupied Dapu. At this point, the important points of Yongchun County were all occupied by Hong's troops. On the morning of the 28th, Zhang's troops abandoned Yongchun and retreated to Dehua. Hong's troops then occupied Yongchun County. Hong Wende also arrived in Yongchun and, on March 1, gathered his main forces, with Shi Baoqi's unit as the vanguard, and continued to advance towards Dehua. The war is unlikely to end easily. It is said that Wei Lihuang has sent personnel to investigate and, after obtaining the truth, will report to the military and political leaders for review. Before the event, the Fifth Route Headquarters received a large number of telegrams from Hong and Zhang mutually exposing each other.

The reasons for the conflict between Hong and Zhang can be explained separately: (1) Distant Cause: During the heyday of Chen Guohui when he served as the commander of the First Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army, he unified Quanzhou and Yongchun, but Zhang Xiongnan of Dehua refused to submit. Zhang was a local gentry in Dehua, occupying Dehua for many years and benefiting from its terrain. Chen entered Dehua several times to attack Zhang, confiscating more than 1,000 weapons from Zhang's troops, but was ultimately unable to eliminate Zhang. When the 19th Route Army entered Fujian and resolved Chen Guohui's troops, Chen was shot in the province. Chen's troops, Peng Tang, Chen Yucai, and Chen Peiyu's three regiments, were surrounded by the 19th Route Army and their weapons were confiscated. They retreated to Shuikou in Dehua, but Zhang cut off their retreat, causing Peng Tang's entire army to surrender their weapons. Chen Peiyu and Chen Yucai also had four-fifths of their weapons confiscated. Zhang obtained 3,000 weapons and more than 20 machine guns, greatly increasing his power. The 19th Route Army divided its troops to surround Zhang, but due to the unfavorable terrain, they ultimately had no way to deal with him. When the Central Army entered Fujian this time, Yang Fengnian incorporated Chen and Zhang's troops into the Minnan Punitive Army, with Hong Wende as the commander of the First Route. Zhang also served as the commander of the Third Detachment, but the two major forces stood side by side and had old hatred, which is why they killed each other. (2) Recent Cause: Zhang occupied Yongchun when the 19th Route Army retreated. However, Yongchun was the fundamental base of Chen Guohui's old troops. When Chen Guohui entered Quanzhou in the past, Peng Tang was stationed in Yongchun for more than two years. Now that the 19th Route Army has been defeated, Peng Tang, Chen Yucai, Chen Peiyu, Liu Chaoran, and others are doing their best to expand their strength, indiscriminately incorporating scattered troops, buying up the lost weapons of the 19th Route Army, and taking in the remnants of the 19th Route Army, Shi Baoqi, Ma Hongxing, and Huang Ying, claiming to have 10,000 people, confined to the corners of Nan'an Jinbei and the border of Anxi, requiring 2,000 yuan in food expenses every day. Zhang Xiongnan also had a large increase in troops, and provisions were waiting to be raised. Both sides set up checkpoints to levy taxes, and conflicts occurred frequently between Nan'an and Yongchun. Peng Tang was stationed in Shishan, which was particularly affected. Recently, dozens of telegraph poles were cut down between Shishan and Yongchun. Peng Tang sent a team to patrol Nanwushi, on the border of Nan'an and Yongchun. Zhang Xiongnan, upon hearing the report, transferred a large force from Xiaohu, and the two sides made contact once. Later, You Sifu's unit, with more than 300 bandits, originally contacted Zhang Xiongnan to surrender, but suddenly changed their allegiance to Chen Yucai, which greatly displeased Zhang and accelerated the opportunity for war. However, both sides still confronted each other between Dapu Penghu and Nanwushi Mountain. On the morning of the 26th, Hong's troops launched an attack, and the war began. Moreover, both sides aimed to gain territory to support their troops. Therefore, how to reduce the number of the huge militia at present, how to provide provisions, and prevent them from acting outside the law are major problems for the aftermath of the Fujian situation. (March 3)

| Punitive Army Will Jointly Attack Ruijin |

Overseas Chinese from Siam Arrive in Xiamen Due to Hardship 92

Report on the Massacre of Overseas Chinese in Siam

Xiamen Dispatch: A group of seven overseas Chinese, including Su Biaoqi, who were expelled from Siam and returned to their homeland, arrived in Xiamen on the 27th of last month. They reported that on October 28th of last year, in the area of Botongpo, Siam, local Siamese famine victims demanded relief from the government, which led to disturbances. The Siamese government used military force to suppress the unrest and indiscriminately shot, imprisoned, and expelled innocent overseas Chinese. At the same time, Su and others submitted a report to the Xiamen Overseas Chinese Association, requesting them to forward it to the central government for relief. The account of the incident by Su and others is so appalling and heart-wrenching that it is recorded as follows:

1. At 12:00 noon on October 28th last year, in Botongpo, Siam, sudden and loud gunfire was heard from the police station. The order in the streets was immediately disrupted, and shops and residences were closed one after another. The disturbance subsided at 4:00 p.m. This incident occurred because a small number of famine victims hoped for relief from the police station, which affected innocent people. A total of 22 people were shot dead, of whom 13 were confirmed to be good overseas Chinese. The names of the other nine are unknown. Later, the massacre continued with the following victims: Zhang Naiqing on the 29th, Ya Jin and Zheng Cheng on the 30th, and Lin Mei on the 31st, totaling 27 people. Before the incident, the Siamese government had detained five overseas Chinese, none of whom had committed serious crimes. When the incident occurred, they were all shot dead one by one. Among the five, Chen Yajiang was from Jiaying, Guangdong, and was accused of private gambling; Lin was from Guangxi and was accused of private wine brewing; Su Chengchun was from Yongchun, Fujian, and no crime was announced; Luo Shiyi and his son were from Jiaying, Guangdong, and no evidence of any crime was heard. It was found that Su Chengchun was a businessman with no bad habits, owning fifty to sixty acres of rubber plantations. He had an elderly mother, a wife, and four children. Luo Shiyi had an eighty-year-old mother, a wife, and three children. His eldest son, nicknamed Luo Bali, was only fourteen years old. Because his father was arrested innocently by the police, he chased to the police station and was also tied up and suffered the same fate. In the afternoon of November 1st, at 4:00 p.m., the authorities led a large group of police officers, fully armed, to spread throughout the streets. They immediately killed Che Shi from Huizhou, Guangdong; Wei Hao from Chaozhou; Fu Quan from Guangxi; five people including the driver of Xinhexing; one a clerk in a Hetu shop; one a Kelai person; and the other three were collecting rubber liquid in the rubber plantation behind the market. The most tragic was Che Shi, who was peaceful and amiable in life. Twenty years ago, he went to Botongpo to run a grocery store, built houses, and opened hundreds of acres of rubber plantations, with assets of about 100,000 taels of gold. He left behind an eighty-year-old father and a widow and young children. In the afternoon of the 29th, the police station summoned Zhang Naiqing to the yamen and shot him without discrimination. Zhang was 28 years old, from Yongding, Fujian, and a student at Tsinghua University in Beiping. In August of last year, he was hired as the principal of the local Chinese school and had only been in office for three months before being killed. On the 30th, Ya Jin and Zheng Cheng were shot dead. Ya Jin was from Guangdong, over sixty years old, and worked in a garden. That morning, he was plowing when he was suddenly shot. Before he died, he was carried to the police station, where he passed away. Zheng Cheng was from Tong'an, Fujian. Before the chaos occurred, he went to the county office for some matter. On his way home, he heard gunfire and fled to a witch's house for refuge. Three days later, when he wanted to return home, he was killed. On the 11th, Lin Mei was beaten to death by the police with gun butts. Lin was ill and had been detained for several days, cut off from food, moaning and waiting to die. But the cruel and inhumane police beat him to death with gun butts. Moreover, on the morning of the 29th, the local county magistrate and police chief led a large group to the streets, arresting anyone they saw, regardless of whether they were farmers, workers, or merchants, totaling 82 people. They were imprisoned in a small room of ten feet in the police station, which was almost impossible to stand in. The crowd was hot and stuffy, like being near a fire. Although they were hungry and thirsty, they were not given white water. The police beat them randomly with gun butts while searching them, filling their pockets with all the money they could find, amounting to about six or seven hundred yuan or more. As a result, more than ten people suffered from sudden illnesses and fever, and the sound of wailing was endless. In the afternoon of the 30th, the police allowed them to drink water after much pleading. On the 31st, the detainees, because they had not eaten a grain of rice and were starving to death, asked the police for food. The police replied, "The officials want to put you to death, do you still want to eat?" In the afternoon, the deputy police chief was on patrol, and the crowd told him that since the officials intended to put them to death, why not shoot them one by one. The deputy police chief was slightly moved. At dusk, each person was given a small package of rice (the amount of a small bowl). These 82 people were imprisoned until November 3rd, when more than 50 people were released. The rest were still tied to the stone pillars at the foot of the police station, all emaciated and almost starving to death. In total, from October 29th to November 4th, 5th, and 6th, Siamese vagrants were brought to the police station every day to falsely accuse them. On November 16th, the 82 people were divided into three groups. The first group consisted of 47 propertyless people who were bailed out by businesses. The second group of 16 people were sent to Songjiao on the 17th to suffer imprisonment. On January 19th, they were transported by train to Bangkok for detention pending trial. On February 3rd, they were sent to Shantou on the Youlishi ship. The third group of 19 people were taken to Danian in three cars on the morning of November 17th and are still being held in the local prison. It is unknown how they will be dealt with.

Chiang Kai-shek Bans Banquets, Gambling, and Opium 93

All Levels of Personnel Should Purge Themselves of Old Evils

Leaders and Officials Should Cultivate Themselves and Set an Example

Hankou Dispatch: Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek, while supervising the troops in Hankou, previously issued an order to the military and political authorities of all provinces to prohibit indulgence in feasting and entertainment. Yesterday, he reiterated the previous order, stating, "It is through adversity that we can survive, and indulgence only invites calamity. Moreover, in the face of internal and external troubles and numerous disasters, we are in a precarious situation. Every time I think of the soldiers on the front lines, their bones exposed on the battlefield, and the countless victims filling the ditches, I find it hard to sleep. Anyone with a conscience should be aware of the impending danger and should be vigilant, diligent, and introspective. However, a comfortable and decadent lifestyle has become a common practice, with endless singing and dancing taken for granted, pursuing pleasure and seeking only temporary security. If this continues, how can we encourage self-improvement and reverse the decline? From the date of this order, all military commanders at all levels and administrative personnel in all provinces shall cease banquets and eliminate unnecessary social gatherings. Moreover, opium and gambling can erode ambition, waste time, and are a great scourge that destroys the country and the family. Strict prohibitions should be enforced and diligently implemented. All public officials should strictly abide by the prohibitions and purge themselves of old evils. Leaders and officials should cultivate themselves and set an example, so as to achieve great benefits through small acts of integrity. Anyone who disobeys in secret will be severely punished without leniency upon discovery." (March 3rd)

Unlicensed Japanese in Jiading Get Drunk and Cause Trouble 94

On the 25th of last month, two Japanese men resembling merchants, carrying guns and without passports, came to Jiading from Shanghai by car. The Snowball Garden in the city is privately owned by the Hu family and is located in a remote western part of the city, rarely visited by tourists. However, it was used as a field hospital when the Japanese army invaded. Some say that the Japanese went there because they were familiar with the local situation, implying that their visit was ostensibly for sightseeing but secretly for political purposes. Later, the Japanese men got drunk in a restaurant outside the East Gate and were escorted to the Nanyang Hotel by police officers. At 10:00 a.m. the next morning, Inspector Yao Lianqun of the Public Security Bureau led police officers to the hotel and politely persuaded them to return to Shanghai. After arriving at the train station, the older one pretended to be drunk and punched someone, refusing to board the train. He then fled into the wilderness, almost causing trouble. The police immediately chased him back and sent them both onto the train. They were still acting crazy on the train, causing alarm to the other passengers.

Taicang Holds Mediation Meeting with Martial Arts Performance 95

A few days ago, several customers, including Li Ganlin, came to Jiang Senmao's restaurant in Xiamenwai, Taicang. Because the heated wine was not exchanged to their satisfaction, they had an argument with the restaurant staff, Shi Shaoqing. Fortunately, they were persuaded to stop. However, Li Ganlin was still unwilling to let it go and gathered dozens of people from the city to meet with Shi and others at the teahouse opened by Zhang Shouzhen for a mediation meeting. Because they disagreed, they threw tables, chairs, and teapots. When the police arrived, Shi Shaoqing, Yang Axi, Ding Gangrong, and two others were seriously injured. The police immediately telegraphed the headquarters, and all the police officers rushed to the scene to suppress the situation. Only then did they stop. Li Ganyao, Gao Zihuo, and six others were arrested and brought to justice. The injured were taken to the county government for examination.

Three Drown in a Capsized Brick Boat in Suzhou 96

Yang Mazi from Hangzhou, who worked for the Sancailong Shipping Company outside Changmen, hired Shen Peisheng's boat to transport a large batch of bricks and tiles from Suzhou to Hangzhou. While passing through Yangcheng Lake, a sudden wind caused the boat to capsize. Of the four people on board, Yang was rescued by a neighboring boat. The boat owner, Shen Peisheng, his younger brother, who was deaf, and an old woman who cooked on the boat all tragically drowned. Two days later, the old woman's body floated up and was first reported to the local court for examination and coffin preparation. The bodies of Shen Peisheng and his brother were recovered on the afternoon of the third day and transported to the court for examination. It was a tragic scene.

Bandits Kidnap a Small Steamer in Wuxi 97

The Licheng Steamer Bureau, located under the Gongyun Bridge in this county, had small steamers running between Wuxi and Cheng counties. Initially, business was very prosperous. In recent years, due to the convenience of land transportation, especially after the completion of the Wuxi-Cheng Highway, passengers traveling between Wuxi and Cheng counties mostly took cars. As a result, the bureau's business declined significantly. In order to develop its business, it established branches in Qingjiangpu, Suqian, and other places, and the business was very good. However, on December 12th of last year, the bureau's Flying Whale steamer, departing from Qingjiangpu, encountered bandits in Yangzhuang (about 18 li from Suqian). All the passengers on board were robbed, suffering heavy losses. Before leaving, the bandits also hijacked the steamer. Recently, the steamer was released by the bandits, but the accountant, Mr. Li, and the old helmsman, Zhou Quangen, have not yet returned to the bureau and their whereabouts are unknown. Mr. Li is from Jiangyin, and Zhou Quangen is 20 years old, from Jinchengwan, Yangming Township, Third District of this county. He comes from a poor family and has an elderly mother, a wife, and two brothers. The bureau has reported the kidnapping to the families of Zhou and Li. After hearing the news, Zhou's family was extremely anxious, with his wife weeping and his children crying, a truly pitiful sight. They have repeatedly sent people to Qingjiangpu and Suqian to inquire, but there is still no news. The other day, they went to Jiangyin to inquire about the truth from the Licheng branch and requested the bureau to ask the public security authorities to rescue the hostages so that the family could be reunited.

Labor-Capital Dispute in Oil Factories 98

This county, once known as a developed industrial and commercial area, is now not only superficially strong but actually weak, but also unworthy of the name. Although there are many reasons for this situation, they are all due to the economic aggression of imperialism. The local industry has been completely eliminated, and the silk industry has also failed, leading to the collapse of the rural economy and shaking the entire economic foundation. As a result, the purchasing power of farmers has weakened. During the planting season, they are unable to afford fertilizer, and the sales of soybean cakes produced by various oil factories have sharply declined. Only the large soybean cakes have some sales to other regions, while the rest are virtually ignored. Last year's operations all resulted in losses. Therefore, at the beginning of this year's operations, the wages of workers were reduced, but the workers did not agree, causing the factories to delay their reopening. Until yesterday, the Hengde and Runfeng factories, which use mechanical power to produce cakes, temporarily reopened, specializing in large soybean cakes. All wages remained the same, but the number of official work shifts was increased to maintain operations. As for the oil factories that use manual labor, such as Yimao and Sanhe, two factories temporarily reopened. The rest have not yet resolved the issue of increasing the number of shifts, so they cannot reopen in the coming days.

Murder Case at Tangyang Bridge in Changzhou 99

Liu Xihua, a farmhand in Tangyang Bridge Township, Eighth District of Wujin County, was beaten to death on the third day of the month. The director of the Seventh Public Security Sub-bureau, upon hearing the news, not only went to investigate but also sent police officer Xu Wenhua to the county prosecutor's office to request an autopsy. Chief Prosecutor Yang Kongxi, upon receiving the report, immediately summoned Xu Wenhua for questioning and approved him to supervise the autopsy by car on the morning of the fourth. He would then proceed with the investigation.

Jiangyin County Government Reduces Local Surcharges 100

In accordance with the telegram from the Department of Finance, the county government convened a meeting of heads of various groups and organizations on the afternoon of the second to discuss the reduction of local surcharges. Secretary Bao, representing the county magistrate, chaired the meeting and decided on the following: (1) There are slight discrepancies between the current land prices and the previously set prices, and they should be changed immediately. The previously set price of 110 yuan per mu for superior paddy fields in the canal region should be reduced to 104 yuan, and the previously set price of 44 yuan per mu for newly cultivated fields in the sandy region should be reduced to 40 yuan. (2) The county's regular and surcharges exceed the 101% limit of land prices by 76,092 yuan. In accordance with the telegram from the Department of Finance, the funds collected for clearing local debts, which were collected at 5 cents per mu for paddy fields and 10 cents per mu for sandy fields, should not be collected again. Also, the survey fee, which was collected at 10 cents per mu, should be reduced to 5 cents, and the road construction mu donation, which was collected at 5 cents per mu, should be reduced to 4 cents. In total, these three items will be reduced by 140,502 yuan. As for the expenses and operating funds of various organizations and groups, which have already been reduced repeatedly, the current situation should be temporarily maintained.

Zhenjiang Security Regiment Ordered to Transfer 101

Xiang Zhizhuang, the director of the Jiangsu Provincial Security Office, recently transferred the First Regiment, led by Regiment Commander Li Shouwei, stationed in Huaiyin, to Suqian, and ordered the Third Regiment, led by Regiment Commander Cao Pang, stationed in Tongzhou, to take over the defense. The Fourth Regiment, led by Regiment Commander Jia Yunshan, originally stationed in Suqian, was transferred to Zhenjiang, and the Third Regiment, led by Regiment Commander Yang Wei, originally stationed in Zhenjiang, was transferred to the Yixing and Liyang areas. After receiving the orders, the regiment commanders complied and took over the defense.

Standard Clocks Established in Four Counties 102

In order to ensure accurate time and facilitate public observance, the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department previously approved a merchant, Zhou Desheng, to contract for standard clocks in Zhenjiang, Wuxi, Suzhou, and Yangzhou, and instructed the local chambers of commerce to work with the county technical directors to determine the number of clocks and the installation arrangements. According to Zhou's subsequent report, a total of four master clocks and twenty-five slave clocks will be installed in the four counties, and he has submitted the drawings. The Construction Department has approved them, signed a contract, and notified Zhou to install them quickly so that the counties can establish unified standard time as soon as possible.

Yangzhou County Government Auctions Off Chun Sheng Pawnshop 103

After the Chun Sheng Pawnshop in Yangqiao Township, Fifth District of the county, went bankrupt, it owed provincial funds that had not been paid. The province ordered the county to seal and auction off the pawnshop's buildings to cover the debt. The county government is now soliciting bids for the purchase of the pawnshop's buildings, which consist of 42 rooms, excluding the counter and furnishings, and more than eight mu of land. The minimum bid is 3,200 yuan. Bids will be submitted by 9:00 a.m. on the 30th of this month, and the bids will be opened at 3:00 p.m. The highest bidder will be the winner. Bidders must pay a deposit of 200 yuan, which will be returned after the bidding, regardless of whether they win or not. The winning bidder must pay the full amount to the county within five days. If they fail to do so, the next highest bidder will be selected as the winner.

Local News

Two Chinese Merchant Ships Collide in the Huangpu River Yesterday Afternoon 104

Wanxiang Slightly Damaged, Zhaoxing Sinks

Passengers and Crew Members Safe

The Sanbei Company's Wanxiang and the Zhaoxing Company's Zhaoxing collided in the Huangpu River near the Huashun Wharf in Hongkou around 1:00 p.m. yesterday. The Zhaoxing sank to the bottom of the river in less than half an hour, while the bow of the Wanxiang suffered minor damage. This is the latest unfortunate incident in the shipping industry. Upon hearing the news, our reporter rushed to the scene to investigate and reports the details as follows:

Wanxiang Returns to Shanghai After Duty 105

The Sanbei Company's Wanxiang had been chartered to transport soldiers of the 19th Route Army from Fujian and Xiamen to Beijing for pre-training. After disembarking the soldiers in Beijing, the ship returned to Shanghai. Yesterday, around 11:00 a.m., it entered the Wusongkou and at 12:50 p.m., while passing near the Huashun Wharf in Hongkou, it encountered

Zhaoxing Leaves Port 106

The Zhaoxing, belonging to Zhaoxing Company, loaded a large batch of flour and miscellaneous grains at the Longmao Wharf in Lujiazui, Pudong, and departed for Yantai and Longkou. It set sail from Shanghai at 11:30 a.m. yesterday. At 12:50 p.m., while sailing near the Huashun Wharf in Hongkou, it saw the Wanxiang coming head-on. At that time, it was high tide, and neither ship could avoid the other, resulting in

A Tragic Collision 107

The Zhaoxing attempted to turn its bow towards the west bank to avoid the collision, but due to the ship's speed and the rapid current, it could not retreat in time. The Zhaoxing's starboard bow compartment below the waterline was hit, creating a hole. River water immediately flooded in. Upon realizing the disaster, the ship's owner immediately sounded the alarm for help. Fortunately, it was daytime, making rescue easier. The Wanxiang's bow also suffered minor damage, but it was not serious. Therefore, it helped with the rescue. In less than an hour, the Zhaoxing sank completely. Only the mast is now visible above the water. Fortunately, apart from the cargo in the cabins, which sank with the ship, all of the

Passengers and Crew Are Safe 108

The Zhaoxing was carrying 14 passengers and a crew of about 50 to Yantai and Longkou. They were all rescued by the water police, the Wanxiang crew, and nearby ships and safely landed ashore. However, all their luggage and belongings were lost.

Estimated Losses of the Zhaoxing 109

The Zhaoxing has a deadweight of 1,200 tons. It was carrying 40,000 bags of flour and over 1,000 pieces of miscellaneous goods, with an estimated loss of about 200,000 yuan. It had been insured with the Zhaotai Insurance Company, but the amount insured is unknown because yesterday was a Sunday, and the company was closed.

Wanxiang to be Repaired the Same Day 110

After the collision between the Wanxiang and the Zhaoxing, the bow of the Wanxiang suffered minor damage. The company helped with the rescue work while sending someone to report to the company. Upon receiving the report, the company immediately ordered its factory workers to repair the Wanxiang. The repairs were completed by 5:00 p.m. that afternoon, and the ship was moved to the Hongsheng Wharf at 6:00 p.m. As for the issue of responsibility for the collision, neither party expressed an opinion yesterday because it was a Sunday. Negotiations will have to be conducted today.

Customs Hangs Warning Signals 111

The customs authorities, fearing that passing ships might mistakenly sail towards the sunken ship and collide with its upper part, dispatched small boats to anchor around the area during the day, flying green flags, and at night, they lit red lights to warn other ships to avoid the area and prevent danger.

Message from the Pilots' Association 112

The General Association of Chinese Merchant Marine Pilots states that the Zhaoxing, belonging to the Zhaoxing Shipping Company on Guangdong Road in this port, had just completed its annual repairs at a Japanese shipyard in Dalian. It was delivered to Shanghai by the Japanese side on the 3rd of this month. It had not yet been inspected by the Shanghai Maritime Administration to determine if the repairs were legal. Due to the urgency to sail, it was loaded overnight with over 1,000 tons of flour and miscellaneous goods and departed from Longmao Wharf at 12:05 p.m. yesterday, heading for Yantai, Longkou, and Tianjin. When it reached the Lujiazui area, it encountered the Wanxiang, belonging to the Sanbei Company, coming from Wusong. At the time, a sugar barge was obstructing the route. The Zhaoxing, in an attempt to avoid it, slowed down and signaled the Wanxiang first. However, the Wanxiang was traveling at high speed and was close to the shore, causing the Wanxiang's bow to collide with the Zhaoxing's forward compartment. The ship, which was smaller and older, was unable to withstand the impact. After about four or five minutes, it was carried by the tide and sank in front of the Jardine Matheson Wharf. Fortunately, the accident occurred during the day, and no one was injured.

French Aviatrix Hélène Boucher Leaves Shanghai Yesterday 113

Flies Directly to Seoul, Then to Tokyo

Will Return to Shanghai at the End of the Week on Her Way Home

French aviatrix Hélène Boucher, who flew her 650-horsepower Blériot land plane on a second long-distance European-Asian flight, arrived in Shanghai at 4:00 p.m. in February and stayed at the French Consulate General on the Bund. After a short rest, she flew out of Shanghai in the same plane at 8:25 a.m. yesterday, bound for Seoul. Here are the details of her departure from Shanghai:

Farewell from All Sectors 114

Around 7:00 a.m. yesterday, Hélène Boucher and her assistant, Bla克斯, traveled to the Hongqiao Airport from the French Consulate General in a car. The French Consul General, 梅理靄, and Consul, 古阿發, were both at the airport to see her off. Yang Hu, the director of the Municipal Security Bureau, sent a representative, 王志成, to lead a small team of motorcycle escorts to the airport to maintain strict security. The political department of the French Concession police also sent personnel to take care of everything.

Flying to Seoul 115

After Hélène Boucher and the farewell party arrived at the airport around 7:40 a.m., they chatted for a while. After the Asiatic Petroleum Company added gasoline to the plane, Hélène Boucher inspected the plane and then climbed aboard. Amidst the rumbling sound of the engine, she shook hands with the farewell party. At 8:25 a.m., with a final "goodbye," she turned the plane's nose, took off, and headed straight for Seoul. The farewell party only left after the plane disappeared from sight.

Returning to Shanghai Next Week 116

Hélène Boucher is scheduled to arrive in Seoul, Korea, around 4:00 p.m. yesterday. Shanghai and Seoul are about 600 miles apart, and the flight should only take seven hours. She plans to stay there overnight and fly to Tokyo the next morning. She intends to stay in Tokyo for a few days and then return to her country via Shanghai. The date of her return to Shanghai is expected to be this Friday.

Not Arrived in Seoul 117

The Japanese Union News Agency reported from Gyeongseong, Korea, on the 4th that the French aviatrix Hélène Boucher, who departed from the Hongqiao Airport in this port at 8:25 a.m. this morning for Korea, has not been seen as of 7:30 p.m. tonight. There is also no news from Tianjin or Qingdao. It is unknown whether she has encountered an accident on the way and is a matter of concern.

China National Aviation Corporation Plans to Shorten Shanghai-Chengdu Route 119

Plans to Purchase a State-of-the-Art Aircraft

Scheduled to Be Implemented This Summer for the Convenience of Passengers and Mail

The Xin Xin News Agency reports that the China National Aviation Corporation, due to the thriving business between Shanghai, Hankou, Chongqing, and Chengdu, and the extremely developed passenger and postal services, plans to use the latest type of aircraft for flights this summer in order to shorten travel time and facilitate passengers and mail. The company is currently planning to purchase the aircraft. In the future, it will be possible to take off from Shanghai in the early morning, arrive in Hankou at noon, and reach Chengdu in the afternoon. At that time, the journey between Shanghai and Chengdu will only take two days, with only ten hours in the air. The postal service will become even more convenient.

Shanghai Business Community to Depart for Shandong for Inspection Tonight 123

Also Plans to Proceed to the Yangtze River and Southwest Regions for Inspection

At the invitation of Shandong Chairman Han Fuqu, a group of Shanghai business leaders, including Guo Shun, Qian Chengxu, and Hu Xiyuan, have organized an industrial inspection delegation to conduct an inspection of industries in the province, with the aim of studying and developing the province's various production industries, and establishing a foundation for talent and economic cooperation between Shanghai and Jinan. Inspection Route 125

Regarding the delegation's inspection route, Qian Chengxu told the reporter that after arriving in Jinan, they will depart in two directions. One group will go along the Jiaoji Railway, ending in Qingdao, while the other group will go directly to Pingjin via the Jinpu Railway. Therefore, their stay in Jinan will be short. After returning to Shanghai, Qian, Cai Shengbai, Hu Xiyuan and others will go to the Yangtze River region, including Jiangxi, Hubei, Hunan, and Sichuan provinces. Guo Shun, Zheng Yizhi and others, at the invitation of the southwestern provinces, will go to Guangdong, Guangxi, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces.

Ministry of Finance Rejects Additional Cotton Yarn Tax Collection in Chongming 126

Referred to Jiangsu Provincial Government for Handling

Chongming County is located at the mouth of the Yangtze River, and its terrain is strategically important. Due to continuous erosion by the river, part of the county has already collapsed. Out of a sense of protecting their homeland, the citizens of the county intend to levy an additional tax on cotton yarn, using the proceeds to prevent further erosion. They had previously submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance for review. However, the Ministry of Finance, considering that the additional tax on cotton yarn would affect the entire tax system, rejected the request and referred it to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for consideration. The details are as follows:

Ministry of Finance Rejects Additional Tax Collection 127

The Ministry of Finance issued a response stating: Received the submission. After the implementation of the unified tax on cotton yarn, all taxes and levies should be exempted. The county's continued collection of erosion prevention donations on cotton yarn that has already paid the unified tax clearly contradicts the regulations on the unified tax on cotton yarn and should be stopped in accordance with the rules. It cannot be compared with taxes on land, small rents, or port fees. Erosion prevention projects are local affairs and should be funded by the provincial government through other means. The ministry has received submissions from citizens of the county, including Chen Jiagu and Yufeng Yarn Mill, and has referred them to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for investigation and handling. Regarding the current situation, in addition to referring it to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for joint handling, you are hereby notified.

Ministry of Finance Consults Jiangsu Provincial Government 128

The Ministry of Finance consulted the Jiangsu Provincial Government, stating: The Ministry has received a petition from Huang Xianlin, standing director of the Chongming Farmers' Association, Li Wenwei, standing director of the Education Association, Ling Lianfa, standing director of the Textile Industry Workers' Union, and Fan Rulin, standing director of the Fishermen's Association, requesting the imposition of an additional tax on cotton yarn to fund erosion prevention. After the implementation of the unified tax on cotton yarn, Yufeng Yarn Mill has repeatedly submitted petitions to the ministry, and the ministry has referred them to your provincial government for investigation and handling. Regarding the current situation, in addition to issuing a response, the ministry hereby consults you for reference and joint handling. Please respond.

Domestic Manufacturers Schedule Shanghai North National Products Exhibition 129

The Chinese National Products Manufacturers Association believes that the dumping of foreign goods is increasing day by day. According to customs reports, the trade deficit in January of this year reached a staggering amount of over 40 million yuan, which is alarming. If we do not actively promote domestic goods and increase production, the national economy will be in a state of bankruptcy. In view of this, the association has joined forces with Shanghai North gentry and businessmen Wang Binyan, Li Zhuxuan, Cai Qiajun, She Xipin, Yuan Hongjun, Li Guangjin, etc., to hold a Zhabei National Products Exhibition to encourage the people of Zhabei to jointly promote domestic products. The association has already surveyed the Datong Road in Zhabei and designated the Zhabei Charity Group as the venue. Preparations are currently underway, and the opening is scheduled for March 15. The details are as follows:

Committee Meeting 130

The association specially convened a committee meeting yesterday for this matter. Those present included Liu Zhongying, Chen Binghui, Jin Weixuan, Cai Qiajun, and more than twenty others. Liu Zhongying presided over the meeting, Zhou Zhaolin took the minutes, and the meeting proceeded as scheduled. The items discussed included: (1) Please confirm the name of the Zhabei National Products Exhibition. The meeting decided to name it the Shanghai North National Products Exhibition. (2) Please confirm the opening date. The meeting decided to open on March 15. (3) Please nominate the preparatory committee. The meeting decided to nominate Xu Yunhui, Chen Binghui, Wang Binyan, Liu Zhongying, Gu Zhuxuan, Cai Qiajun, Gu Wensheng, Yuan Hongjun, Cao Zhigong, She Xipin, Hu Xiyuan, Ren Shigang, Xi Guansheng, Sun Xinzhu, Jin Weiyi, Zhang Shengai, Lin Guyun, Tao Zigun, Li Guangjin, Zhang Lixing, Cai Mingzheng, and others as preparatory committee members.

Filing for Record 131

The association specially filed a request with the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau for record, stating that the application is for holding the Shanghai North National Products Exhibition, requesting approval and registration for the benefit of the proceedings. Foreign goods are being dumped more and more every day, and the outflow of money is uncountable. If this continues, not only will domestic goods factories be in danger of collectively shutting down, but the national economy will also be on the verge of collapse. The root cause is that the Chinese people are chasing after foreign goods and despising domestic goods. If this inferiority complex of valuing foreign goods and despising Chinese goods is not eradicated, then domestic goods will never be able to flourish. Based on this purpose, the association is committed to promoting domestic goods, and the National Products Exhibition is the most important and practical way to promote them. At the request of the majority of members and factories, the association plans to hold the Shanghai North National Products Exhibition to give the people of Shanghai North an opportunity to recognize domestic goods, so as to arouse their awareness of using domestic goods. The Zhabei Charity Group on Datong Road in Zhabei has been designated as the venue, and a temporary business site will be attached to the venue for the public to purchase goods. In addition to submitting an application to the Social Affairs Bureau for registration, the association hereby submits a written request to your department for review and approval, so as to facilitate the proceedings.

Notice to All Factories 132

Notice: It has been decided by the committee meeting to hold the Shanghai North National Products Exhibition. The Zhabei Charity Group on Datong Road in Zhabei has been designated as the venue, and the opening is scheduled for 1:00 PM on March 15. The location is convenient, and the market is thriving, making it ideal for exhibiting domestic products. You are hereby notified that we hope your factory will join us as soon as possible to make the event a success. There are not many booths available, so register as soon as possible to avoid missing out. The registration office is located at No. 160 Baker Road, the association's office.

Chen Qubing Memorial Service Held Yesterday 134

Wu Tiecheng Presided, Ye Chucang Represented the Central Government to Offer Sacrifices

The death of Chen Qubing, a prominent historian of the Southern Society and member of the Party History Compilation Committee, was commemorated by important figures from the Party and State, as well as his former colleagues and friends, at a memorial service held at the Ningbo Fellow Provincial Association at 3 PM yesterday. The details are as follows:

Order of the Assembly: (1) Sing a memorial song, (2) Representative of the Central Party Department offers sacrifices, (3) Representative of the Judicial Yuan offers sacrifices, (4) Representative of the Southern Society offers sacrifices, (5) Representative of the Autumn Society offers sacrifices, (6) Representative of the Jingxiong Girls' School offers sacrifices, (7) Representative of the Wujiang Shanghai Fellow Provincial Association offers sacrifices, (8) Students offer sacrifices, (9) All attendees of the memorial service offer sacrifices, (10) Chairman of the preparatory committee delivers a eulogy, (11) Report on the life of Mr. Qubing, (12) Speeches, (13) Family members offer thanks, (14) Adjournment.

Attending Representatives: Attendees included Ye Chucang, representing the Central Party Department, Tan Zhen, Vice President of the Judicial Yuan, Cai Yuanpei and Wu Zhihui, members of the Central Committee, Ju Zheng, President of the Judicial Yuan (represented by Liu Xialing), Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai, as well as Pan Gongzhan, Li Dachao, Liu Yazi, Hu Puan, Yao Yuping, and representatives from the Southern Society, Autumn Society, Wujiang Shanghai Fellow Provincial Association, Jingxiong Girls' School, etc., totaling more than 600 people. The service was presided over by Wu Tiecheng.

Chairman's Address: Chairman Wu Tiecheng gave an address, saying, "Members of the Southern Society initiated the memorial service for Mr. Chen Peiren and entrusted Tiecheng and others to be responsible for the preparations. Today, not only old friends from this city have taken time out of their busy schedules to attend, but many have also traveled from afar to be here, which shows the deep respect of people in society for Mr. Chen. Looking back, after the success of the 1911 Revolution, much of the credit goes to the power of written propaganda, and Mr. Peiren was one of the most diligent people at that time in using writing to promote the revolutionary movement. Although Mr. Chen was a scholar, he used writing as a tool for revolution, but he also took practical action on many occasions. His articles, morals, personality, and career are not only admired by the members of the Southern Society but will also be forever engraved in the hearts of people across the country. Many of you present here today are old friends from the Southern Society and are very familiar with the history of Mr. Peiren. I will only say a few words based on my personal feelings. Mr. Chen was one of the most powerful participants in the revolution. He worked hard during the initial rise of the revolutionary forces, and he never slackened even after the revolution was completed. This is one point that makes us admire him. He was extremely devoted to his friends, and if someone entrusted him with something, he would do his best to accomplish it. As for his family, this is the second point that we admire him for. At this time, I feel even more that the old comrades in the Party are gradually aging and gradually passing away, and the national affairs are also getting worse day by day. Therefore, we old friends are extremely saddened by Mr. Chen's death, and thinking of the efforts of the old comrades in the past, we feel even more saddened by the current state of national affairs."

Ye's Report: Ye Chucang, representing the Central Government, then reported, "All of you present here today are either old friends of Mr. Chen or his students, so you know a lot about Mr. Chen's death, and the history of Mr. Chen's revolution is even more known to everyone at home and abroad, so there is no need to repeat it. What I want to say is that we all know that Chen was a revolutionary scholar, but we do not know that Mr. Chen also repeatedly participated in the actual work of the military. When I was eleven or twelve years old, it was after the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895. At that time, people in the country all wanted to avenge the shame of the Sino-Japanese War. However, Mr. Chen believed that if we wanted to avenge the shame of the Sino-Japanese War, we must first avenge the shame suffered by our nation more than 260 years ago. Therefore, he immediately recruited comrades and organized the Xuechi Society, which was actually a revolutionary organization. Mr. Chen also tried his best to bring a powerful army led by Fei into the society, which aroused suspicion from the outside world and eventually failed. From this, we can see that Mr. Chen not only made written propaganda but also made far-reaching military preparations. Another time, I spent New Year's Eve in Zhouzhuang (a rural area in Suzhou), and Mr. Chen came in a hurry and left in a hurry before dawn. Later, I learned that Mr. Chen took advantage of the opportunity to seal the customs and secretly transported military supplies to a secret military organization in the countryside. The above two things were actual work of the national revolution, which was ten years before the founding of the Republic of China, when the Southern Society had not yet been established and I was still studying in a rural school. This small amount of information is of irreplaceable value. In addition, Mr. Chen often liked to talk about national affairs with his friends, often until all night. He would also earnestly teach and guide the younger generation who asked for advice and never got tired. I have been working in propaganda for a long time and know that the deepest influence on people must be a gentle and generous heart. Mr. Chen was a person who possessed this character. From this, we must recognize that Mr. Chen was a scholar who was also capable in the military, an old predecessor who liked to encourage the younger generation the most."

Speeches by Wu and Cai: Then, Wu Zhihui, Cai Yuanpei, and others gave speeches in succession. Wu said, "Mr. Cai Jiemin and Mr. Chen Peiren and I are all old friends, so I know them very well. Most people in the world today think that Chen is a scholar, but I don't think so. Mr. Chen did not use writing as a tool for entertainment but to exert his ability to lead the masses. It is not only in the propaganda of writing, but also in actual work. We should not regard the success of Yao, Shun, Wen, and Wu as not being scholars, and the failure of Confucius, Mencius, Lao Zhuang, Mo, and Xun as being only scholars." Cai said, "I want to contribute two points of view at today's memorial service. First, the function of writing has a great and lasting influence, and establishing a name can especially pass on people to immortality. Mr. Chen used his whole life to promote the function of writing, so we must collect his posthumous works today to commemorate Mr. Chen. Second, the life of a person is limited, but the life of a group is infinite. Although Mr. Chen did not enjoy a very long life, he passed away suddenly, but his spirit can be entrusted to the group to pass on to infinity, such as the Jingxiong Girls' School and the Southern Society founded by Mr. Chen. Therefore, I hope that the members of the Southern Society will be able to work hard to extend the Southern Society to infinity, because extending the life of the Southern Society is also extending the life of Mr. Chen." The rest of the speech was omitted.

A Glimpse of the Funeral Odes: Among the elegiac couplets, there was Lin Sen's plaque "Tongde Minggao" (Exalted Reputation), Chiang Kai-shek's plaque "Xiuwen Fuzhao" (Pursuing Studies and Responding to the Call), Wang Jingwei's couplet "Longxing Shi Nanxun, Nanshe Jiuren Tui Zijian" (The Dragon's Nature is Difficult to Tame, Old Members of the Southern Society Recommended Zijian), "Pengyu Tian Suoe, Wujiang Fengyu Zhu Yu Bei" (The Peng Island is Restricted by Heaven, the Winds and Rains of Wujiang Helped My Grief), Yu Youren's couplet "Ying She Qin Tongfu" (Responding to the Society and Admiring Tongfu), "Gaofeng Xi Zhonglian" (Admiring Zhonglian's Noble Demeanor), Chiang Kai-shek's couplet "Guo Shang Duo Jian Shence Qimou Si Dengyu" (The Country is Still Difficult, Thinking of Deng Yu's Wise Strategies and Ingenious Plans), "Tian He Bu Yin, Zhiji Doujiu Ku Qiaoxuan" (Why Doesn't Heaven Have Compassion, Crying for Qiaoxuan with a Chicken and a Pot of Wine), Li Liejun's couplet "Jiubing Shijiang Zi Qiangu" (Wine, Soldiers, and Poetry Have Been Around Since Ancient Times), "Wenyuan Rulin Gong Yichuan" (Literary Garden and Confucian Forest Share a Biography), Kong Xiangxi's couplet "Zaosui Du Yinfu, Kuang Ju Yun Yu Longzhonglue" (Reading the Yinfu Sutra Early in Life, Planning to Live in Seclusion and Making Great Plans), "Zhuangyou Bian Yinghai, Zhang Ce Shi Can Weiwo Mou" (Traveling Around the Seas in Youth, Sometimes Participating in Tent Campaigns with a Staff), etc., totaling four or five hundred pieces.

Memorial Text of the Assembly: On March 4th, the twenty-third year of the Republic of China, all members of the memorial service respectfully offer clear wine and a variety of delicacies to the spirit of Mr. Chen Qubing, saying, "The ten thousand acres of Lake Taihu are truly blessed with spiritual beauty. The Pine and Pottery River and Marsh gave birth to our honorable gentleman. The family has a tradition of chivalry, with lofty aspirations like Zhu and Guo. The two Chens are distinguished, with high vision and foresight. Our honorable gentleman was orphaned early and depended on his mother. With the appearance of a dragon and the demeanor of a phoenix, he was a scholar but not pedantic. There was an elder scholar in Wu, named Xu Xianglu. He taught in the River and Fen area, a teacher of scriptures and a teacher of people. The door displayed high rankings, with two willows twice. Our honorable gentleman came out late, daring to follow Jin. In the year of Jiawu, the new flame was extinguished. In the year of Wuxu, there was reform. Kuaiji was ashamed, and lectures gathered the group. In the year of Guimao, he went east to Japan. To resist the Russian army, he raised a knife and slapped the tent. Where the wind and clouds went, to resist the barbarians and reject the Manchus, with bare hands, he swore to raise the Han banner. He struck the alarm bell and built the stage. The surviving people recorded it, and secret history suffered disaster. The literary network was highly visible, and he walked around Anhui and Zhejiang. After Xu Xilin was martyred, he followed in Nanyue. He mourned the ancients at Yai Mountain, with tears filling his eyes. He returned across the sea, and ulcers grew on his left elbow. The illness was finally cured, and he lived in seclusion in Gaoqiao. He then founded the Southern Society, and the national soul could be summoned. The three gentlemen stood as tripods, namely Gao and Liu. He recorded thousands of people, and his writings were eternal. The Xinhai Restoration was splendid and bright. He raised the great Han banner and lived in Canglang. He floated on the Xiang River and waded through the foothills. He traveled to Wanping. Shi Heng entered Luoyang, and ten thousand streams of hearts poured in. He had great thoughts and distant visions, crossing over Juyong. He planned the border and settled the far away, watching the sky dreamily. He protected the law in Guangdong and assisted Sun Zhongshan in planning in the tent, listening to his words and following his advice. He swore an oath in Shaozhou, with the Yellow Dragon wine full. Who would have thought that Chen Jiongming would eventually betray the Han? He returned to his lofty aspirations, putting down his arms and focusing on literature. He lectured at Tai Xue, on the bank of the Yangtze River. But heaven did not have pity, and the beams broke and the rafters collapsed. He escorted the coffin south and returned, with the soul of a loyal subject broken. He chose a tomb in Zijin, truly building it himself. The master craftsman transported the axe and consulted and measured. It was the year of Yangjiu, and Luoyang and Sichuan were in turmoil. He矫尾厉角, 左袒環龍. After the southeast was settled, Wu and Chu merged. A cry at Zhaoling, and grudges and grievances were all wiped out. The strong have already been rewarded, and the Peng map is temporarily suppressed. He典藏新京, 修史焦麓. Time does not stay, and the green jade and blue Yao are quite close to the beginning of smelting. One autumn night, the moon violated Shaowei. The jade coffin suddenly descended, and the women cried and the children wailed. Tracing back to the birth of the honorable gentleman, the rivers and mountains are like the sun and stars. Grieving the death of the honorable gentleman, the lingering shadow of the snake. On the Bin of Wusong, thinking of the honorable gentleman's old travels, the old friends are in the hundreds, and the high society is celebrating with drinking. Green pines and cypresses, setting the public spirit well, yellow bananas and red lychees, beckoning the public soul. There is meat in the sacrifice, and there is wine in the bottle. May you come down here, and bless and enjoy." Then, Liu Yazi, the representative of the Southern Society, respectfully offered a piece of incense and a thousand lines of hot tears to the spirit of the Choonam Mengchang, saying, "Alas, at the end of the Qing Dynasty, the sky was stinky and the sky was fishy. I raised the Southern Society to resist the Northern Court. We, the Chaonan Society, were the first to set up a big flag. There was also Tian Mei, with the left horn and the right corner. The thief was incompetent, but he was still in a tripod. He looked at the sky with white eyes, with tears filling his eyes. For thirty years, the sea has turned into a mulberry field. Tian Mei died early, and the public later passed away. Facing the flute and the yellow furnace, a cry in the west wind. Old friends have fallen, auspicious unicorns and mighty phoenixes.
