Jiangsu Provincial Farmers' Bank Establishes Agricultural Marketing Office in Shanghai 136

Office Located in Nanshi, Operations Commenced

In recent years, the rural economy has fallen into bankruptcy, attracting widespread attention. The root cause is, of course, the low price of agricultural products and the inconvenience for farmers in direct marketing to urban markets. Therefore, merely injecting financial resources without focusing on the marketing of farmers' products cannot fundamentally resolve their livelihood issues. Recognizing this, the Jiangsu Provincial Farmers' Bank has established the Jiangsu Provincial Cooperative Agricultural Marketing Office in Shanghai. This aims to provide continuous support to farmers from the seedling stage to the sale of harvested grains. It is reported that the office's objective is to exclusively act as an agent for the marketing of products produced by various cooperative societies and farmers throughout the province. The preparatory office has already commenced operations, located at No. 3, Peide Lane, Lima Road, Nanshi. The director is temporarily concurrently held by Mr. Hou Houpei, deputy manager of the Farmers' Bank head office, and the deputy director is Mr. Hu Duming. The office's regulations for agency marketing and purchasing are excerpted below: (1) According to Article 2, Section 2 of the organizational charter, the office may act as an agent for cooperative societies or farmers to purchase fertilizers, seeds, and other essential production materials. (2) When entrusting the office to make purchases, prior consultation and a detailed written commission, in a format prescribed by the office, are required. (3) When entrusting the office to handle goods, the trademarks, types, prices, and other details must be clearly specified in the written commission. Otherwise, the commissioning party will bear responsibility for any errors, returns, exchanges, or other losses. (4) When entrusting the office to purchase goods, the office may charge a handling fee proportionate to the value of the goods, but not exceeding 10 per mille. In special circumstances, the fee may be calculated based on the volume. (5) When entrusting the office to handle goods, the principle is to prepay a corresponding amount (interest-free), with any surplus refunded and any shortfall to be made up. When necessary, the office may introduce the commissioning party to the Jiangsu Provincial Farmers' Bank to borrow funds against the entire value of the goods. (6) If the market price is unsuitable, the prepaid payment will be fully refunded, and the handling fee may be partially or fully returned. (7) All shipping costs, taxes, and other expenses incurred in entrusting the office to purchase goods shall be borne by the commissioning party. If necessary, the office may advance payments, and the interest will be calculated daily according to the Shanghai interbank rate. Upon receiving notification from the office, the commissioning party shall immediately prepare funds for repayment and must not delay. All advanced payments and interest shall be calculated in Shanghai silver dollars. (8) Upon receiving the delivery notice from the office, the commissioning party shall immediately pay all outstanding amounts and present the receipt to collect the goods. If the goods are not collected after the deadline, the office may sell them. (9) When necessary, the commissioning party shall insure the goods. The office can act as an agent for insurance, and the insurance premium shall be borne by the commissioning party. (10) The office is not responsible for any accidents if the goods are not insured by the commissioning party or cannot be insured, or if they have been declared but not yet insured. (11) The price of all goods purchased on behalf of the commissioning party shall be based on the invoice. (12) If goods cannot be shipped immediately after purchase, the office may store them in a warehouse without seeking the commissioning party's consent, and the warehousing fees shall be borne by the commissioning party. (13) After the goods have been shipped, postal delivery will be based on the postal receipt, and shipping by sea will be based on the bill of lading. The office is not responsible for any incidents that occur en route but may jointly investigate with the commissioning party. (14) These measures may be amended at any time if there are any omissions. (15) These measures will be implemented after being approved and promulgated by the head office of the Farmers' Bank.

Interruption Discovered on the Nanjing-Shanghai Railway Track Between Changzhou and Xinzhazhen 140

Fortunately, a Slow Train Passed

Emergency Dispatch of Engineers for Repair

The 12th third- and fourth-class slow train from Shanghai to Nanjing on the Nanjing-Shanghai Railway at 9:25 AM yesterday discovered that the track was interrupted by more than a foot at the 169-kilometer mark between Changzhou and Xinzhazhen stations at approximately 4:00 PM. Fortunately, it was a slow train with a lower speed, so no accident occurred. Upon safely arriving in Xinzhazhen, the train conductor immediately reported the situation to the stationmaster. Upon receiving the report, the stationmaster immediately detained the 9th express train from Nanjing to Shanghai yesterday afternoon. At the same time, he urgently telegraphed the Changzhou Engineering Section to report. The engineer stationed in Changzhou, together with the stationmaster of Changzhou Station, supervised the workers to carry tracks and ride a single locomotive to repair. The work was completed at 6:30 PM, and the 9th express train departed from Xinzhazhen again. Therefore, the train arrived in Shanghai last night about an hour later.

Lawyer Association's General Meeting Yesterday Adjourned Due to Lack of Quorum 141

The Shanghai Lawyer Association convened a temporary general meeting of members at the Lake Society on the second floor of the Beijing Road intersection in the Public Concession yesterday (Sunday) to discuss amending the association's charter. From 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM, members Shen Junru, Wang Weizhen, Chen Tingrui, Dong Chi, Mao Yun, Yu Zufeng, Liu Mingdu, Liu Xiang, Yao Jian, Yao Wenshou, Lu Shaozong, Yu Zhongluo, Shan Yuhua, Shi Qinghua, Wu Zhengque, Chen Zhigao, Lu Dingkui, Lu Dingming, Qin Liankui, Zhang Xiongfei, Peng Qixiu, Li Yuan, Guo Wei, Zha Renwei, Huang Zengjie, Zhong Shilin, Huang Yan, Xue Jiaqi, Bian Jialu, Zhou Yu, Wang Xiaowen, Zheng Wentong, and others, a total of one hundred and fifty-nine people, arrived successively. Lima Road Shoe Store Tragedy: Mother and Son Buried Together in a Fire 145

Decorating the Lantern Festival with Paper Lanterns Leads to Catastrophe

Unable to Wake Them in the Emergency, Resulting in Being Burned to Death

At approximately 2:00 AM yesterday morning, the Chen Yuji Shoe Store at No. 66, Yangjiadu Heng Street, Lima Road, outside the Dadongmen in Nanshi, suddenly caught fire. A tenant mother and son were burned to death on the spot, and five houses were destroyed. Details are recorded below.

Years of Operation 146

The Chen Yuji Shoe Store was opened by Chen Shuxing from Jiangdu and has a history of several years. The business is considered relatively prosperous. Chen's wife, Guan, is 23 years old and has a one-year-old son named Hongzi. The whole family lives in the front building of the house. The back building is rented to his younger brother, Shumo. The pavilion is rented to a Mr. Gao, and a three-story loft is rented to Pu Changfa, a fellow villager who is a dockworker.

Decorating the Lantern Festival 147

Chen's younger brother, Shumo, is 23 years old. He married a Miss Wang last summer. Recently, as the Lantern Festival of the old lunar calendar approached, city residents are accustomed to hanging paper lanterns indoors as decoration. Chen was no exception. Chen lit the lantern and hung it by the bed the night before. However, at approximately 2:00 AM yesterday morning, the red candle burned out, burning the entire paper lantern. In an instant, the curtains were all ignited, immediately starting a raging fire. Chen and his wife were awakened in shock, but it was already irreparable and impossible to save.

Catastrophe Occurred 148

In an instant, the flames had already spread to the upstairs, breaking through the roof. The fire brigades from various districts drove pump trucks to the scene to connect water for extinguishing. In addition to the complete destruction of the store's building, its neighbors, No. 64 Gu Shunxing Bamboo Mat Store, No. 62 Zhang Tongxing Hemp Bag Store, and the building of a certain Mr. at No. 60, as well as one façade of No. 58 Yuanxing Cigarette Paper Store, were also affected and almost completely destroyed. The total losses are significant.

Mother and Son Die Together 149

It is believed that when the fire was raging, Pu Changfa (55 years old), a dockworker from Yangzhou living in the store's three-story loft, his wife, Wu (59 years old), and his son, Dengbao (37 years old), were sound asleep because they worked hard during the day. Therefore, they did not notice the fire downstairs at all. Subsequently, the flames spread to the loft, igniting the cotton quilts that Pu and others were covering. Pu Changfa woke up from his dream, but saw that the room was full of flames and was very panicked. He immediately called out to his wife and son to get up quickly.

Fire Starter Arrested 150

It turned out that after calling out several times, they still did not wake up. At that time, Pu's shoulder had been burned by the flames and was unbearably painful. Therefore, he did not have time to put on clothes and jumped down from the loft naked to escape to the outside of the door, which allowed him to escape the danger. However, his elderly wife and beloved son could not be saved. He could only witness the two of them being buried in the fire. At that time, Chen Guan, the starter of the fire, had been arrested by a policeman from the first district and taken to the first district along with Pu Changfa. After first giving Pu clothes to wear, he was immediately sent to the hospital by car. The district chief, Guan Gong, interrogated Ms. Chen once and then ordered her to prepare a document and send it to the bureau for further interrogation. He also sent people to the fire scene to dig out the bodies of Pu's wife, Wu, and his son, Dengbao. However, both corpses were burned beyond recognition, with broken heads and rotten faces, and intestines flowing out, which was extremely tragic. Yesterday morning, District Chief Guan ordered the local Jia to report to the Shanghai Local Court and requested that personnel be sent to conduct an autopsy today.

Exquisite Smoking Tools Used by Upper-Class People

The Asia Hotel, located at No. 135 Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession, was previously found by the French police to be harboring gambling, and the Vice Captain Xie Guangming, Hang Bingquan, and detectives Cai Zongyi of the gambling arrest team were dispatched to search it. Unexpectedly, in addition to hotels allowing gambling, they also allow people to privately set up opium dens inside, providing people with lamps to smoke opium. The mechanisms are tight, and it is not easy for outsiders to know. On the evening of the second, the detectives of the French police gambling arrest team learned that someone was gambling in the hotel and rushed to search it at 0.15 points. The gamblers had already escaped when they heard the news. The detectives searched the rooms one by one and found the smell of opium emanating from the front of Room 518 on the fifth floor. It was discovered that there was an opium den inside. After knocking on the door for a long time without opening, only the sound of footsteps was heard in the room. When the waiter was called to get the key to open the door and enter, the opium lamp was brightly lit on the bed, and the furnishings were extremely luxurious. The opium smokers had already escaped from the window or the mechanical door in the toilet behind the bed. Only Hua Daxin, a native of Yong (28 years old, formerly a compradore on a certain steamer of Taikoo Company), who privately set up the opium den, was arrested. Two smoking guns, four lamps, four pipes, fourteen taels of opium paste (including the jar), another box of thirty-one five-tael opium bubbles, a jar of ash, sold for fourteen yuan, one large and one small iron box, countless sundries, ten decks of dominoes, a box of Hua's business cards (printed with Asia Hotel, Room 510, Seafarers' Office), and two opium account books were seized. From the smoking tools seized, it was speculated that the addicts who went to smoke and eat were all upper-class people. Hua and the evidence were taken to the police station. After questioning, he admitted to privately setting up the opium den. When the detectives came to search, there were Wang and Zhu smoking inside. When they heard the knocking, they escaped, etc. The police chief ordered them to be detained. The next day, he was sent to the Criminal Court 1 of the Second Special District Court. The police lawyer Fei Xizhen explained the case and presented the evidence to the court. Then, the bailiff Cai Zongyi reported the search process. When Hua Daxin was questioned, he confessed that the opium den was opened by Wang Yichang, who was at large. I went to find a friend to entrust a job in the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and was detained. After Judge Zhang Zhaoyou examined the opium account book among the exhibits, he ordered the defendant to write numbers and compared them with the handwriting on the account, which matched. When the defendant was questioned again, he finally bowed his head and admitted to privately setting up the opium den. The court then sentenced Hua Daxin to eight months in prison and a fine of two hundred yuan. The fine was commuted to one day of imprisonment for every three yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment was confirmed was used to offset one day of imprisonment for every two days. The seized smoking tools and other items were confiscated, and the defendant was detained in the detention center pending instructions.

Capital Increase of One Hundred Twenty Thousand Yuan Completed

Regular Shareholders' Meeting Scheduled

The Silk Industry Bank of Sanma Road has enjoyed a strong reputation and made significant progress in its business since its opening. A board meeting was held yesterday (the 3rd), attended by Zhang Danru, Xu Ji[name], Dong Lan[name], and over ten other board members. Chairman Wang Yansong presided over the meeting and reported on and discussed several important matters, which are disclosed as follows: (A) Matters Reported: (1) The number of various savings deposits received by the bank's savings department and the savings section of the Eight Immortals Bridge branch in the past two months has increased sharply, indicating that the bank's service to society is becoming increasingly widespread and that the public's trust in the bank is growing stronger. (3) The renovation of the Hangzhou branch is nearing completion and is scheduled to open in the middle of next month. The Nanshi branch is scheduled to open on the 20th of this month. (B) Matters for Discussion: The bank's capital increase, as approved by the previous shareholders' meeting, set the increase at 400,000 yuan. However, due to the excess, it was changed to a capital increase of 600,000 yuan. Although this was resolved by the board of directors, according to Article 186 of the Company Law, this capital increase, exceeding the amount approved by the previous shareholders' meeting, should still be submitted to the shareholders for approval. In addition, the bank's profit distribution over the years should also be submitted to the shareholders' meeting for approval. It was decided to schedule the third regular shareholders' meeting, in accordance with Article 19 of the bank's articles of association, to be held on April 5th at the Bank Association. It is reported that various matters are being actively pursued.

The Ancient Bronze Ding Transported to Shanghai Has Been Sold 162

A Shanghai Collector Purchases It for a High Price

The ancient bronze ding transported to Shanghai from Shouzhou, Anhui Province, was confirmed by Shanghai archaeologists to be an antique from before the Three Dynasties. The Ministry of Education also sent a telegram to the Shanghai Education Bureau to investigate. It has been learned that the ding has been purchased by a Shanghai collector for a high price. According to the owner, the ding was buried deep in the ground, over sixty feet deep, surrounded by wooden boards on all sides. When it was unearthed, the wooden boards were already badly rotted. It took over six months and more than one hundred workers to excavate the ding. Therefore, the owner's expenses were considerable. When unearthed, there were many animal bones inside the ding. It is said that these bones were the so-called "animal charcoal" used for burning incense in ancient times. There are many antiques in the counties around Shouzhou, Anhui Province, but unfortunately, they have been scattered in various places. It has been learned that the owner has completed the sale and will soon be leaving Shanghai.

Shen Enfu Reviews Introduction to Shuowen Books 167

Six Books of Justice...Shuowen Key...Shuowen Key Sequel

Mr. Ding Junzhongyou immediately printed Shuowen Gulin and its sequel, the culmination of the government's study of Xu Xue, so that small scholars could originally examine each character and study the theories of various schools. Recently, he compiled and printed three kinds of "Six Books of Justice", "Shuowen Key" and "Shuowen Key Sequel", so that beginners can get the ladder to entry. Mr. Shen Xinqing recently read the three books, deeply admired Mr. Ding's diligence, and especially congratulated young people with national studies. The special features are as follows: ("Six Books of Justice") Among the six books, the two meanings of transformation and borrowing have the latest inventions. The example of borrowing in Xu's book is based on the theory of Gaomi, and it is correct to say that the wrong words written in Shuowen Xuchuan have a basis, and they are by no means created by imaginary ones. ("Shuowen Key") Using the circumference method, from shallow to deep, it attracts people, and the various articles of the official script change, and all those that do not conform to the original meaning of the word creation are collected and listed, which can save the scholar's examination of the eyes, ("Shuowen Key Sequel") collecting Shuowen's questions and answers, and the study and proofreading of the words in Shuowen's classics. Two types can help in the study of the classics. One type of ancient literature is that all common words that are not found in Shuowen can be seen at a glance. Its name is called Key, which can be said to be true to its name. In fact, all three are the keys to Shuowen. If scholars want to see the halls of Xu's book, they must first ask to enter the common gate, and if they want to enter the gate, they must first get the key.

Diamond News Fined 168

Accused of Publishing a Satirical Cartoon

After the Ji Juemi was sued for raping Xu Yuying, Diamond News published a satirical drawing in the newspaper. The picture shows two doors, and a person is drawn making an entry. The word "law" is written on the door, and the word "Buddha" is written on the person's back. On both sides of the picture, the words "Yamen Hall opens and no money comes in", "No bystanders allowed" and "Backdoor entrance and exit" are written. It was discovered by the First Special District Court Procuratorate that the newspaper had published this cartoon, which was suspected of insulting the public office. The newspaper's editor, Zheng Yimei, was summoned to the case by Prosecutor Zhong Qing, and after the interrogation, it was deemed that a public prosecution should be filed. Zheng was ordered to pay a bail of 500 yuan, and the lawsuit was filed in the same-level criminal court in accordance with Article 146, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday, Judge Wu Xiangzu opened a court hearing. Prosecutor Zhong stated the reasons for the prosecution in court, and the defendant Zheng Yimei also hired a lawyer to defend himself, saying that the illustrations published were satirizing the An Guan Temple and the old yamen. Finally, the prosecutor presented his arguments, and the judge then declared that the defendant was found guilty of publicly insulting the public office, and was fined 300 yuan, and two copper plates of the Diamond News and one copper plate were confiscated. During the appeal period, the defendant was still on original bail.

Trainees Sent to Austria by the Ministry of Communications to Register in Beijing and Shanghai Starting Today 174

Postal Savings Employees and University Graduates Can Apply

The Ministry of Communications, recognizing that China's postal savings and remittance businesses are still in their infancy, and for the sake of future development, urgently needs to send personnel abroad for practical training to learn from experience and improve. However, the Ministry was hesitant about which country to send them to. After careful consideration, it was decided to send them to Austria, as Austria's postal savings business is the pioneer in the world, and all rules and regulations are more complete and superior than other countries. The Ministry has now finalized the recruitment regulations and will begin registration simultaneously in Beijing and Shanghai from today (the 5th) to May 15th. The examination will be held in Beijing on June 1st. (Registration procedures can be found in the recruitment regulations.) The quota is set at six people. Candidates must be current employees of the postal and savings and remittance bureaus, as well as university graduates who have worked in banks. In addition to the Ministry providing all tuition and miscellaneous fees, there are also excellent benefits.

Fire at Fuyou Road Foreign Jade Store 177

Fire at Yu Ming Spreads to Five Stores

Zhu Jiachun Missing, Arson Suspected

Shen Zhenhua, the head of the First Branch of the Second District Public Security Bureau, upon receiving orders, immediately moved to crack down on foreign jade workshops and was in the process of ordering the owners of said workshops to sign pledges and install fire-fighting equipment within a set time limit. Unexpectedly, yesterday at 10:00 AM, a fire broke out at the Yu Ming Foreign Jade Store at 306 Fuyou Road. Due to the nature of the raw materials used in foreign jade, which are made of rosin, it can easily ignite if one is not careful, and it spreads extremely quickly. Police officer Cui Bingyan of the No. 2 post spotted it and immediately returned to the station to report it. Chief Shen, in addition to notifying the fire brigade, personally led Inspectors Qi and Hong, Police Chief Ma, and others to the scene to maintain order and assist in the rescue. However, the fire had already spread to five other businesses on the same road: the Yong Xing Foreign Jade Store at 304, the Ma Hong Xing Foreign Jade Store at 308, the Yong Xing Zhai Foreign Jade Store at 310, and the Hua Mei Glassware Store at 312, all of which were engulfed in flames. Fortunately, it was during the daytime, and no one was injured. The fire was extinguished after about an hour. Afterwards, Chief Shen, finding that the owner of Yu Ming, Zhu Jiachun, was out, had no choice but to detain Zhu Huian, the store's junior manager, for questioning. Zhu Huian confessed that he was from Danyang, 20 years old, and that the Yu Ming Foreign Jade Store was established by his father, Zhu Jiachun. This morning, his father had gone to a teahouse for a cup of tea and had not yet returned. He was upstairs when he heard the apprentices say that a mishap occurred when they accidentally spilled chemicals during work, causing the disaster. Chief Shen found Zhu Huian's statement vague and was unsure of the cause of the fire or whether there was insurance. As the store owner Zhu Jiachun could not be found, arson was suspected, and he was sent to the bureau for interrogation. Meanwhile, the police were ordered to investigate the true cause of the fire.

New Medical Techniques for Postpartum Complications Postpartum fever is notoriously difficult to treat. The Zhengdao Layman in Shanghai has promoted massage therapy, which has shown remarkable results in treating difficult cases. It is even more miraculous in treating postpartum conditions. Last autumn, in August, the wife of Director Huang Jintao of the Hankou Tax Collection Office had postpartum bleeding and abdominal pain two days after giving birth, accompanied by chills and fever. All doctors were ineffective. Later, she was admitted to the International Hospital in the city for treatment, which lasted for over eighty days. Her illness had weakened her, and she was in an increasingly dangerous state. A foreign doctor diagnosed that she would be in danger within three days. Fortunately, the layman rushed to Hankou and applied massage therapy, which resulted in her recovery. Generally speaking, this condition is mainly treated by draining the accumulated fluid. It is said that in Mrs. Huang's case, not only was the blood clot drained, but a large amount of mineral fluid was also discharged with the urine. The fluid was white, shiny, and hard, forming grains. It was different from the various white powders seen in ordinary urolithiasis or kidney deficiency, or other conditions of kidney weakness. Many obstetric experts have studied it and believe that they have never seen anything like it. It is truly a new medical technique for postpartum complications.

Reading Q&A

Reading and Writing 186

Sir! My previous plan for allocating these two hours of time for reading was as follows: From 8:00 to 9:00, I would read (either literary books or social science books); from 9:00 to 10:00, I would write an essay. The reason why I have not achieved any results with this plan is, first, because, as you said, I lack the "seriousness" of study in reading. Although I myself often realize that "it is not good to read without seeking deep understanding" and not to appreciate the exquisite artistic essence of the book, I have tried reading a book three or four times. However, the result is not only that I do not get a deep impression, but also that the interest fades, like beer that has lost its fizz. I have also read many new literary books and four or five social science books, but what remains in my mind is only a vague impression, especially in social science. However, when reading these books, I believe that my spirit is still focused, and there is probably not much that I do not understand. However, the impression I get is only this, which cannot help but make me feel disappointed, as if I have been splashed with cold water. Is this because my brain's memory is weak, or is it something else? Is there any way to remedy it? Now I have made a new reading plan: the most important thing is not to read a lot, but to seek the essence of a certain model book. For social science books, I have chosen "Sociology from a Materialist Historical Perspective," published by Beixin in 1930. For literature, the long stories are "The Slaughterhouse," and the short stories are blank, "Education of Love," and favorite essays in "Free Talk." I have read a few pages of the former, and I roughly understand the meaning. I only read half of it at the time. Now, when I advocate rereading it, I will read at most one chapter per day and take notes after reading each chapter, in the hope of getting a clear concept. Is this correct? As for literature, I advocate not limiting the time and flipping through it at any time, but studying its syntax, structure, such as description, etc. I hope that you can instruct me on a method of exploration.

Second: I have the ambition to create, but my ambition is not great. I only hope that I can achieve a general standard of smooth writing and be able to express myself at will. Judging from my current level, I don't know how far I am from that goal. But my desire to write is very strong, and every day I want to pick up a pen and write. Because I am not good at selecting and discarding materials, and I don't know how to describe them, my writing is very slow. Although I have the ambition to write every day, the result is that I can't write a short article for dozens of days because I want to write every day. I myself know that the cause of this problem is that I have not formed a complete and comprehensive whole of what I want to write in my mind, but only a vague impression. So when writing, I write this point, and then forget another point; some places are not thought of in advance, but are written unconsciously; sometimes, when I write halfway, I feel that I can't continue writing, so I read the written text to evoke the mood of the following text. So my writing is completely done while writing and thinking, and I have never finished writing in one breath. As a result, my drafts are always heavily revised and must be rewritten repeatedly (that is, this letter I am writing is also the case). This unnecessary loss in time really makes my heart ache! What makes me even more heartbroken is that I have spent extremely precious time and energy, and what I have written is not just the arrangement of words, but is completely lifeless, as rigid as a clay Buddha. And after practicing writing until now, not only is this habit difficult to change, but there is still no progress. Sometimes I am so depressed that I hit my head repeatedly, vowing that I will never write again. However, my desire to write is too strong. As long as a day passes, the unstoppable enthusiasm will tell me to sit down and write calmly. But when I see people writing, they can write it out at once, without deleting or changing a single word. It looks like a very easy and quick thing. And the writing is so thoughtful and the layout is so meticulous, which I can never do. How much I admire and regret myself! Sir! You are a person with literary cultivation and professional writing skills. I hope you will not hesitate to use your valuable experience in writing to guide me on how to improve this bad habit!

Furthermore: After reading the essay I attached, do you think my hope of being able to achieve a general standard of clear writing and express myself at will is not great? What about the descriptive sentences and structure in this text? I hope you will take the trouble to give me detailed instructions, which will be of great help to my future writing! (Letter from Wu Hesheng)

Spring and Autumn

Displaying Beauty and Offering Ugliness 190

— Feng Zi

Beauty is welcomed by everyone, while ugliness is detested by everyone. Even a three or five-year-old child, when praised for their beauty, will have their young heart stirred with pleasant waves. How much more so for adults who are involved in society. However, beauty is not something everyone possesses; it belongs to a very few. Ugliness, on the other hand, occupies a vast territory within the population. Because beauty is so rare, its status is all the higher, and the welcome it receives is even stronger. Clever people in society, if they have no beauty to find in themselves or to display, will always try to conjure up some beauty to exchange for glory. But if, unfortunately, they have ugliness instead of beauty, they will be anxious and unable to sleep, urgently seeking ways to remedy the situation. If there is no way to think of, they must at least hide it! Otherwise, to suffer a lifetime of shame would be extremely foolish, wouldn't it?

The boundaries between beauty and ugliness are certainly different, and the nature of beauty and ugliness is also not fixed. In oneself, there is beauty and ugliness in appearance and body, and beauty and ugliness in decoration and expression. In the environment, there is beauty and ugliness in reputation, and beauty and ugliness in status. The former mostly belongs to women, while the latter mostly belongs to men. Women want beautiful faces, curved bodies, and modern and up-to-date decorations and expressions. Men want pure reputations and high status. Only then can they generally receive special welcomes and preferential treatment. Conversely, all kinds of unexpected contempt, abandonment, and even unforeseen disasters will befall them. Oh, beauty, what a priceless treasure to hear about.

Although the boundaries between beauty and ugliness described above are clearly different, they can also be accommodated and borrowed from each other. For example, actors on stage can play female roles as men, putting on an act, and male prostitutes in big cities can temporarily act as night attendants, applying rouge and powder. Self-respecting, naturally handsome men can at least take the lead in certain situations. Women can also use similar tricks. If they are born ugly and cannot be helped, they might as well speculate on their reputation, write a few poems, write a few articles, and put up the sign of a priority—Miss; then with the glorious title—female poet, female writer, they won't have to worry about no one bowing down to them.

So-called status has no inherent beauty or ugliness, but people with status, whether male or female, can compensate for it even if everything else about them is ugly. Don't you see how old men with high status can win the sympathy of modern girls? So the function is the same!

Casual Talk in Cartoons

The Child's Mother 191

— (Written by Qian Yun) (Drawn by Dong Liang)

The husband's wife, A Da's mother, perhaps is too healthy, giving birth to a son as easily as laying an egg; however, she is too busy, dressing the child in the morning, preparing breakfast for the husband, and then, with her large belly, going to the small vegetable market; after returning, she tells the neighbor's wife at the door that the new store sells four catties of meat, so cheap!

After eating, five hundred shovels is her enjoyable work, with her belly resting on the edge of the table. When she can't draw the tiles, the neighbor's wife, unafraid of fatigue, often teaches her; A Er plays marbles on the muddy ground, A Er learns to smoke cigarettes, A Da has a fight with the neighbor's child; she only feels annoyed and scolds, "Little murderers!"; what's important is: get rich, "Pong!"

This wife is indispensable to her husband, but is this kind of mother needed by the children, by society?

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 192

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Five: Shedding Tears, He Bids Farewell to His Family to Return to Distant Garrison; Wind and Sand Permeate the Night as He Leaves the Border to Station in a Lonely City

However, the regimental commander urged me to return like this, there must be news from the front. Under these circumstances, it's probably not the time for soldiers to bring their families. He thought heavily, unknowingly the car had already arrived at Xizhimen, and the passengers got off one after another, only then did he wake up. From the long-distance bus to the tram, from the tram to the train, from the train to riding on the back of a beast, a shadow always lay across his heart, it was Gui Zhi's eyes filled with tears, yet a smile on the corner of her mouth. In a windy and sandy day, he rushed to Xifengkou. The sun was obscured by the wind and sand, and no sunlight was seen on the road. The sky was filled with a color that was neither yellow nor red. The northwest wind blew past from the sky, whistling. For people who are accustomed to living in the northern continental area, such a windy and sandy day is not considered anything special. But in this place, it was somewhat different. From afar, he saw the Great Wall, stretching like a long line on the peaks of the high mountains, rising and falling, faintly revealed in the wind and sand. Looking back and thinking of the great Beijing, the familiar seaside, the sweet home, this made one lose the courage to go forward. But he, as if drunk and enchanted, only recognized one road and walked forward, always continuing to walk. They were a group of people stationed in an old camp in the pass. Zi Qiang arrived at the regimental headquarters, seeing the regimental flag planted by the roadside outside the gate, the two guards with guns on their backs, and the heavy gray-white gate courtyard walls, all the desolate and tragic scenes were in his eyes, feeling that this trip home to get married was like a dream. He dismissed the porter and carried his luggage back to the company headquarters. Sergeant Wang Shili saw him coming, saluted, then shook his hand and said: "Company Commander Zhao, you came really fast. I thought you would only arrive tomorrow morning, I didn't expect you to arrive today." (327)

Neglect 193

— Chen Qi

Every time I run into a friend's or relative's home, I always end up eating lunch or dinner there, and I always hear the polite words "Sorry for the poor hospitality" from my friends and relatives, especially the women.

This is China, where politeness is everywhere, and impoliteness can also be seen everywhere.

Walking on the road, you can see fellow Jiangbei brothers colliding with each other while vying to be the first to cross when the green light turns on, even breaking out into curses, even though it's all for the sake of getting to their destination first.

Speaking of "sorry for the poor hospitality," it is indeed a very common polite phrase, but from this, we can understand the solemnity of ancient etiquette and the respect for guests.

But upon closer reflection, it becomes contradictory.

If you are a poor friend, then it's not like that. The moment you step into the door of a friend or relative, every face will look at you with anger, as if you are their enemy, or they might even avoid you as if they were afraid of ghosts. At that time, you will really feel embarrassed to death.

If you want to cadge a meal, that's even more of a torture. Either they will ignore you, or they will give you a dead face. Then, not only will you not hear the words "sorry for the poor hospitality," but you will at least hear a few cold words, and what you receive will definitely be the real "neglect."

So, to receive the words "sorry for the poor hospitality," you must also have the appropriate qualifications!

Furthermore, when people have a celebration and invite you to a feast, with plenty of meat and fish, in the end, you will also hear the polite words "sorry for the poor hospitality" from the host. But please note that it is exchanged for a cost of at least two yuan.

Gambling 194

— Shi Chun

There is a famous gambling city in the world, a public den of gambling, which many people probably know without saying is Monte Carlo, the gambling city of France. The curious American film industry even made a movie a few years ago, set in the gambling city, called Monte Carlo, which shows that the gambling city's reputation has spread to all countries in the world.

Some people have said that there is also a Monte Carlo in the East, and that is our Shanghai. Whether Shanghai is the Monte Carlo of the East, that is for others to judge, and we don't need to say much. However, the matter of gambling is indeed very popular in Shanghai. Although it may not be as grand as Monte Carlo, it can still be counted in comparison. Monte Carlo relies entirely on gambling revenue to cover municipal expenses. Shanghai has never done so, which may be the difference between Shanghai and the gambling city? Gambling is indeed a very strange thing. Many large hotels and inns in Shanghai, as soon as you enter, you can hear the sound of slapping tiles. These many places are really no different from small-scale "Monte Carlos." However, this seems to be a more civilized form of gambling. Otherwise, this great city of the East would really be in chaos and become Monte Carlo the Second.

It is not known when gambling first began. In our country, the trend of gambling has a very long history. What we know is that in ancient times there was a gambling tool called chupu, which was probably popular for a time. Until now, all gambling is generally referred to as chupu, or sometimes called "yezi xi" (leaf game). So the gambling tool of chupu was probably a kind of playing card, also called "bose." This gambling tool was most popular before the Tang Dynasty, because it is known from historical records that Yang Guozhong, the brother of Yang Guifei, once presented chupu to Emperor Xuanzong of Tang. After the Tang Dynasty, the Song, Yuan, and Ming dynasties all had prohibitions against chupu, so it can be seen that the people of ancient times never did not gamble, and they never did not like gambling, which led to the court's prohibition. Ma diao was also a kind of ancient gambling tool, which some people think is the current mahjong, but in fact, mahjong only became popular in various places after the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom. Speaking of mahjong warfare, it was actually invented by Hong Xiuquan. During the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom, the Heavenly King occupied Jinling, and at that time the city was surrounded by Qing troops. The gates of the city were closed and no one went out. After a long time, there was a stalemate. There were fields in the city of Nanjing, so there was no fear of food shortages, and thus they were able to withstand the siege. However, the city was very lonely and there was nothing to do, so mahjong was invented to pass the time. Originally there were only one hundred and eight tiles, using the one hundred and eight heroes of Liangshan as the card faces. Later, twenty-eight tiles were added, thus creating the current one hundred and thirty-six tiles.

Family Entertainment 195

— Pei Yu

If you are holding a banquet in your home and there are many guests, as the host, you must think of some novel and interesting entertainment methods to make the guests feel interested and endlessly happy. Otherwise, even if you try your best to entertain and be very attentive, only talking and chatting, walking and sitting, eating and drinking, singing and dancing, it will always be dull and not lively. Here are a few suggestions for readers, which I hope will be welcomed.

Biscuit Race

This is a team game with a competitive nature that does not require musical performance; it is also one of the most interesting and convenient entertainment methods at banquets. The method is as follows: divide the guests into two teams, each team having the same number of people, and standing in two rows facing each other. Assuming that each team has ten people, then the host and hostess each take a basin with ten biscuits in it, and stand opposite the first person on the left of each team. After everything is ready, the team members participating in the competition put their hands behind their backs, are prohibited from extending them forward, and are not allowed to whisper to each other or talk at will. The host or hostess gives the order, shouting "one, two, three." After the shout of "three" stops, the host and hostess each pick up a biscuit from their basin and put it into the mouth of the first person on the left of the team to let him eat it, then pick up the second biscuit, move one step to the right, and stand in front of the second person in preparation. When the first person on the left sees the biscuit in his mouth, he quickly chews, the faster the better. After the biscuit is chewed, swallowed, and finished, he turns his head to the right and opens his mouth to the second person; at this time, the host or hostess should quickly put the second biscuit into the mouth of the second person. After the second person finishes eating, he takes care of the third person in the same way as the first person. Eating in this way from left to right in order, the team that finishes eating first is the winner.

Telephone Number

This is also a very interesting competitive game. At least ten people are required to participate in the competition, and another person is the caller and recorder. The ten participants are divided into two teams on average, standing opposite each other, with a distance of more than ten steps between them. Beforehand, the host should prepare twenty white cards of similar size and hardness to playing cards, divided into two sets. Each set of white cards has the numbers from zero to nine: that is, the first white card has a "zero" written on it, the second has a "one," the third has a "two," the fourth has a "three," the fifth has a "four," the sixth has a "five," the seventh has a "six," the eighth has a "seven," the ninth has a "eight," and the tenth has a "nine." Another piece of white paper and a pencil are prepared for recording scores, managed by the caller and recorder. Each team takes a set of number cards, and distributes them to their own team members. The numbers should be in order from left to right, that is, the first person on the left takes the "zero" number, and the last person takes the "nine" number. Each person should hold the number card with both hands, placing it in front of their chest, with the number facing outwards, secretly remembering it, and is not allowed to peek at it temporarily. After they are assigned and standing in order, the caller and recorder takes out a telephone directory and randomly selects a number without the same digits, and shouts it out loudly. For example, if the number called is five, seven, three, nine, then the people holding these numbers in the two teams walk forward two steps, arrange themselves in order according to the telephone number, and face left. The team whose members form a line first and without errors wins one point. After the caller and recorder records the score, the people who stepped out of the line return to their teams in order. If it is planned to hold five competitions, then after the competition is over, the team with the higher total score is the winner.

Charades

This game is most suitable for places with few people. First, divide the guests into two groups. One group stays indoors, called the guessing group; the other group goes outside, called the acting group. They take a few minutes to discuss a phrase with few words that can be expressed with actions. After agreeing, they return to the room together, and each person makes different actions. For example, if the phrase agreed upon by this group is the two words "decoration," then the members of this group, after entering the room, explain to the guessing group that it is a two-word phrase, and then make actions. They might rub their faces and pretend to pat on powder; or loosen the buttons of their clothes, pull and wave, and re-button them, making a gesture of putting on clothes; or step one foot on a chair and tie the laces of their leather shoes tightly; or comb their hair with their hands; and so on, to let the guessing group see and guess. If the guessing group cannot guess what the phrase is within three minutes, then the acting group withdraws from the room again, discusses another phrase, and comes back to perform again. If this time the guessing group guesses correctly, then the guessing group goes outside to discuss a phrase, and comes back to perform, letting the group that was acting guess. In this way, you guess and I act, I guess and you act, taking turns. It is very interesting.

Both Sides Use New Players, Performance Diminished

Tung Wah Forwards Still Sharp, Returning with Victory

The second meeting between Tung Wah and Jinan in the Western Union Group A football match, which was quite noticed by the general public, resulted in Tung Wah defeating Jinan 3-0, avenging the humiliation of losing to Jinan 2-0 last time. Both sides, due to the fatigue of the battle the day before, supplemented their lineups with new players, but the Jinan forwards were inferior to Tung Wah, so the offensive was not as sharp as Tung Wah. For most of the ninety minutes, they were under the pressure of Tung Wah. However, yesterday's battle was very refreshing and watchable. Both sides were very able to abide by sportsmanship, which is a rare and auspicious sight in Chinese competitions in recent years. In the first half, Tung Wah took the lead with a score of 2-0. In the second half, Jinan's counterattack was ineffective, and they lost another goal. In total, Tung Wah won with a score of 3-0.

After the opening kick by Center Forward Li, Tung Wah immediately adopted an absolute offensive. Li Yichen commanded Jia Wan, pressing forward step by step. Gu Shangxiang rescued dangerous balls twice. Wan Xianghua and the others attacked the Zhujiazhuang three times, going straight down the wing, with the force of a rapid wind and rain. Chen Chunxiu and Zhou Honglun served the country with courtesy, causing Jia Youliang to take the opportunity to pick and send to the central position. Li Yichen unleashed his fast legs and charged towards the goal. Little Lai fell sideways, but still could not avoid this disaster, and thus the record was opened.

Chen Hongguang Opened Fire from Afar, Tung Wah Scored One Goal. After Tung Wah scored a goal, the momentum became even more fierce. Although Gu Shangxiang was able to act as a mainstay, it was a pity that one tree could not support a building. Therefore, Jinan's defense was chaotic and dangerous. Zhou Honglun and Chen Chunxiu, two elite soldiers, were under siege on all sides and had difficulty flying. Zhou Guangzhong was like a lion playing with the ball, using all his skills. Wan Xianghua took every opportunity to drill through, and was indeed a dangerous person. Luo Haiguang still thought of borrowing strength from behind the city, but unfortunately the blocks were not the right people, giving Tung Wah an opportunity instead. Chen Hongguang took a shot from 25 yards, rolling into the net, making it 2-0.

Jinan's Counterattack Was Ineffective. After the break, the positions were switched. Luo Haiguang and Gu Shangxiang commanded the large and small armies, preparing to destroy this morning's food. The momentum of the attack was like ten thousand horses galloping. Liu Shizan's feet were stiff, and he was unable to achieve anything when he had the opportunity. What could be done? Zhang Hongzao was close to the goal, but still returned empty-handed, causing the audience to sigh endlessly. At this time, Ding and Wu, the two midfielders, had been ordered to withdraw to the third line of defense. Zhou Xianyan's business was booming, accepting adversity. Within twenty minutes, he played with the ball like a moon, fortunately without any major disasters occurring.

Yichen Created a Straight Three. Although Chen Gongyu came from Tung Wah, his foot was surprisingly hard. With a bang to the head, the ball flew over half the field. The Tung Wah forwards were active again. The two defenders, Chen and Zhou, were unable to stop them, and corner kicks were often forced. Fortunately, Little Wan's feet were soft and weak, and he was unable to wield the knife and go straight in. Until the last three minutes, Li Yichen mixed into the tiger's mouth and swept across, Lai Zuo Rong could not escape this robbery, and thus lost with a score of 3-0.

Group A Billiards Competition Opens, Shen Lince Plays 199

Opponent Bourke

Afternoon 5:30 PM and 9:00 PM Two Games

China Football Club Nan Jin Wins Football Group Championship 201

Wins Over Lingnan 1-0 in Extra Time

Lingnan Fails on Two Penalty Kicks

The final of the China Football Club's Football Group, Nan Jin defeated Lingnan 1-0 yesterday to win the championship. The two teams met at the China Football Field at 11:00 AM yesterday. Lingnan won a penalty kick once in each of the upper and lower halves, but surprisingly failed both times, which can be said to be very fortunate for Nan Jin. When the time ran out, the two teams were tied at 0-0 with no win or loss. As a result of the 20-minute extension, Nan Jin's left winger Miao Zhongqian scored a goal, thus determining the victory.

A Total of Twenty-Two Runners Completed the Entire Course

Careful Selection of Music Teaching Materials and Prohibition of Popular Music in All Schools 209

The Ministry of Education, according to the report from the Music Academy, believes that the cultivation of national morality is crucial to psychological construction. Psychological construction depends on the promotion of aesthetic education, and music is the key to spiritual education. It is requested that all provincial and municipal educational and administrative organs separately inspect the music teaching materials in various schools and prohibit popular music (lewd lyrics and tunes) in society to benefit music education. The Ministry of Education believes that the music teaching materials in all primary and secondary schools should use the textbooks approved by the Ministry. In addition to issuing orders for strict supervision, it also ordered the formulation of measures to prohibit the implementation of effective implementation, and report the handling of the situation for future reference.

Statistical Data on Education in Zhejiang Province in the 21st Year 210

The statistical data on education in Zhejiang Province in the 21st year has been compiled and published by the Department of Education last month. It is divided into five parts: statistical data on various types of education, primary education, secondary education, higher education, and social education. The following are excerpts of the important items for reference by researchers of education in this province.

(1) Primary Education: Number of schools: 12,221, an increase of 485 schools compared to the previous year; number of students: 713,048, an increase of 29,447 people compared to the previous year; number of teachers and staff: 30,407, an increase of 1,243 people compared to the previous year; amount of funding: 5,184,008, an increase of 150,463 yuan compared to the previous year.

(2) Secondary Education: Number of schools: 129, an increase of 7 schools compared to the previous year; number of classes: 678, an increase of 20 classes compared to the previous year; number of students: 22,550, an increase of 585 people compared to the previous year; number of teachers and staff: 2,633, a decrease of 85 people compared to the previous year; amount of funding: 2,370,015, an increase of 143,449 yuan compared to the previous year.

(3) Social Education: Number of public schools: 2,398, an increase of 686 schools compared to the previous year; number of classes: 3,972, an increase of 865 classes compared to the previous year; number of students: 90,930, an increase of 27,761 people compared to the previous year; number of teachers and staff: 5,924, an increase of 1,571 people compared to the previous year; amount of funding: 119,386, an increase of 37,076 yuan compared to the previous year; number of public education centers: 107, an increase of 12 centers compared to the previous year; number of libraries: 46, an increase of 5 libraries compared to the previous year; number of public sports fields: 17, an increase of 6 fields compared to the previous year; number of reading rooms: 2,757, an increase of 499 rooms compared to the previous year; number of public literacy centers: 7,576, an increase of 3,225 centers compared to the previous year; number of public tea gardens: 190, an increase of 106 gardens compared to the previous year; number of parks: 53, an increase of 8 parks compared to the previous year; number of concerts: 69, an increase of 47 concerts; number of sports associations: 64, an increase of 50 associations; number of martial arts halls: 13, an increase of 6 halls; number of public clubs: 9, which are newly established this year.

(4) Educational Funding: The total educational funding for the province is 2,273,025 yuan, a decrease of 566,213 yuan compared to the previous year. The total educational funding for counties and cities (excluding district, township, and private funds) is 3,325,51 yuan, an increase of 305,365 yuan compared to the previous year.

Primary Education in Jiangxi Province Severely Affected by Banditry 211

Only 210,740 Students in the Entire Province

The counties in Jiangxi Province most affected by banditry are in southern and western Jiangxi, followed by eastern Jiangxi, and then northern Jiangxi. Therefore, the eight counties in southern Jiangxi, including Yudu, Xinfeng, Xingguo, Huichang, Shangyou, Ningdu, Ruijin, and Shicheng, the two counties in western Jiangxi, including Yongxin and Ningguo, and the five counties in eastern Jiangxi, including Guangchang, Zixi, and Hengfeng, have been devastated by bandits to the point where education is practically non-existent. Education in neighboring counties has also been affected. According to the general situation of primary education in the 21st year, the statistics show that the total number of primary schools in the province is 5,184, the number of classes is 12,657, the number of male students is 170,146, the number of female students is 40,594, totaling 210,740 students, and the number of teachers and staff is 12,094.

International Geographical Congress to be held in Warsaw in August 212

The International Geographical Congress, which last met in Paris, France in 1931, decided that the next meeting will be held in Warsaw, Poland in August 1934. The subjects to be discussed at the meeting will be divided into the following categories: cartography, physical geography, human geography, prehistoric geography, history of geography, and geographical research methods. For detailed information, please contact the Secretariat of the International Geographical Congress at 6 Rakowieka Street, Warsaw, Poland.

Local News

Sharp Decrease in Student Enrollment at Various Universities This Semester 217

Due to the Social Economic Downturn

Since the beginning of this semester, according to an investigation by the Shanghai News Agency, the number of students enrolled in various universities in Shanghai has decreased significantly. Guanghua University, Fudan University, and Great China University have all experienced a decrease of 100 to 200 students. Chih Tze University, which has both day and night classes, originally had over 600 students, but this semester's enrollment is less than 400. The number of students registered at the College of Political Science and Law and Jiangnan College is also lower than in the past. Even the Law School of Soochow University has experienced a decrease of about 30 students. The reasons for the decrease are complex, but the primary reason is the social economic downturn, which has made it difficult for families of high school graduates to afford the cost of higher education. The number of students in various middle schools in Shanghai has also decreased significantly compared to last semester.

Acting President of Jinan University, Shen Pengfei, Addressed All Students 221

Pay Attention to the Cultivation of Moral, Intellectual, and Physical Education

Foreign Languages to Add Local Dialects of Southeast Asia

If Funds are Available, an Agricultural College Will be Established

Since Shen Pengfei became the acting president of National Jinan University, classes have begun on February 26th and make-up exams will be held starting today. President Shen is actively reorganizing the university. Yesterday, he issued a letter to all Jinan University students, as follows: I, Pengfei, was ordered to serve as the acting president of this university at a time of student unrest and general anxiety. Externally, we are under public scrutiny; internally, there are countless issues to be addressed. Moreover, being an incompetent person, I deeply fear failure. Fortunately, you students are well-read and understand reason. You know the importance of academic studies and recognize the need for discipline. Together, we have worked together to maintain order and restore normalcy. At the beginning of the second semester, lectures have resumed, and society is somewhat relieved. This is truly gratifying. However, the path to order and chaos is often separated by a narrow margin. For example, when managing silk, it is difficult to find the end of the thread after it has become entangled. But if you find the key, it is like the butcher解牛 (庖丁解牛), and everything can be solved easily. Also, like weaving, the thread and yarn are already in place, but if you are careless and break the spool, it will inevitably scatter immediately and cannot be recovered. Therefore, it is very difficult to seek order from chaos, but it is extremely easy to cause chaos when things are already in order. I, Pengfei, am mindful of the戒履霜 (the caution of treading on thin ice) and fear that things that are already in order will easily become chaotic. Therefore, at the beginning of this semester, I dare to sincerely guide you on the key to managing chaos and explain it to you students. The sages have said, "Things have roots and branches, affairs have beginnings and ends. Knowing what comes first and what comes later is the path to virtue." Although this seems like empty talk, it contains profound truths. If we can recognize our duties and do our best in the work that we should do, then although the tasks may be different, the results will be the same. This is why some people have recently proposed the idea of national salvation through fulfilling one's duty. Now, you students have come to this university from afar, either from Southeast Asia or from across the mountains and seas. The purpose is nothing more than to study and prepare for the world.

Those who seek knowledge　are fundamental. Sensual pleasures and the enjoyment of personal rights are all secondary. If we abandon the fundamental and pursue the secondary, there will be chaos. Therefore, the key to managing this is to do our best, study diligently, and not cause trouble or disrupt order by arguing over strict enforcement, heavy workloads, or excessive supervision. Any actions outside the norm should not be repeated. As for school administration, the responsibility lies with the authorities. If students have any opinions, they may express them directly for consideration. However, gathering crowds to make demands or show coercion, forming bad habits, and affecting the school's atmosphere will not be worth the losses, even if they gain something. The reputation of a school depends on the quality of its atmosphere. You students have limited years in school, but you have a long time to be in society. Once you graduate and enter society, people may discriminate against you because you come from a school with a bad atmosphere. The value of momentary excitement cannot be compared to the losses you may suffer. The purpose of establishing a school is to cultivate talents. All facilities should follow this path and aim to make the environment suitable for learning. Although this school has a special mission, its method of cultivating talents cannot be different from that of general schools. We must pay attention to

The Cultivation of Moral, Intellectual, and Physical Education. Consider the Chinese overseas who have traveled far to foreign countries, opened up wastelands, and struggled in lands with harsh climates. They must have special qualities to cope with the environment. During the time when European powers invaded the East and engaged in colonial expansion, they competed for the right to rule. They emphasized the rule of law to impose sanctions, but ritual and education were never promoted. Now, if we want to promote our country's inherent culture and instill it in foreign lands, we must ensure that our overseas Chinese children and those aspiring to engage in overseas Chinese education are thoroughly imbued with both traditional and modern morality. Sun Yat-sen promoted the Three Principles of the People and, at the same time, encouraged people to be loyal, filial, benevolent, loving, trustworthy, righteous, and peaceful. He must have known that both traditional and modern education are indispensable. Therefore, I hope that we can promote the spirit of the nation by sharing the above eight virtues with you students. Speaking of intellectual education, the research and teaching of academics are the main purposes of the school. However, the meaning of learning is diverse. Some are driven by the pure desire for knowledge, while others aim to learn for practical application. It depends on the individual's personality and the needs of the environment. At a time when the country is declining and the world economy is in a downturn,

Learning for Practical Application　should be emphasized by students. Therefore, the school's future policy should follow this goal. In addition to the literature and history courses in the Faculty of Arts, which are the main learning areas for promoting our country's inherent culture, the geography courses are the foundation for developing industries, and the education courses are needed to train teachers, full attention should be given to them. Regarding the Department of Foreign Languages and Literature, we plan to gradually increase the courses in various local dialects of Southeast Asia within the possible scope to adapt to the actual needs of various parties. The various courses in the Faculty of Science should focus on practical science so that they can be linked to various industries of the overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia. The Faculty of Commerce should focus on industrial and commercial management, international trade, and banking courses, with the main goal of being able to obtain practical applications. If funds are available, we will establish an agricultural college, focusing on the education of agricultural and forestry management in Southeast Asia and the Northwest, to help Chinese people go overseas or overseas Chinese return to their country to cultivate and manage. This is the main point. As for physical education, in addition to focusing on maintaining the school's past reputation, we should strive to enhance

Sportsmanship　and promote etiquette, and encourage the development of universal health and physical fitness. For military education, in addition to having sufficient training in academic subjects, we should also focus on cultivating discipline, spirit, and teamwork, and encourage each other to achieve results, so that we can achieve the goal of physical and mental well-being. I have been at the school for less than a month, and I have been distracted by personnel matters and dealing with various affairs. I have not had time to plan the administrative and academic work in detail. Now, at the beginning of the semester, I would like to share my thoughts on the overall situation with you. If I have any further insights, I will publish them at any time to encourage you students.

Cai Yuanpei Praises it, Saying, "Love Students with Virtue, Perfect Students' Beauty"

The Diligence Bookstore at 392 Labor Shenfu Road, Shanghai, has hired thirty-one educators from across the country to co-author a revised edition of the "Student Guide" book. The content is exceptionally rich, and the compilation is exquisite. Mr. Cai Yuanpei's inscription praises the book, saying, "Love students with virtue, perfect students' beauty." There are also prefaces by Zhou Fo Hai, the Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, and others. The entire book is a thick volume with five hundred pages, divided into two volumes. The first volume begins with Ma Chonggan's "Editor's Remarks." The second volume includes twenty articles: Wang Sui's "Science Guide," Sun Benwen's "Society Guide," Tang Qingzeng's "Economics Guide," Gao Jiansi's "Public Education Guide," Jiang Wenyu's "Vocational Education Guide," Wang Xishen's "Sinology Guide," Shen Yizhen's "English Guide," Yu Jifan's "Art Guide," Hu Boxiang's "Painting Guide," Wu Yunrui's "Physical Education Guide," Jiang Xiangqing's "Sports Guide," Lu Lihua's "Dance Guide," Zhong Zitong's "Music Guide," Du Dingyou's "Library Science Guide," Liu Linsheng's "Translation Guide," Wang Yugang's "Hygiene Guide," Zheng Tonghe's "Extracurricular Activities Guide," Pan Yangyao's "Reading Guide," Yang Weiyu's "Entrance Exam Guide," and Liu Zhanen's "Career Guide." The book has many features, and it is particularly accurate in detailing research methods and guiding cultivation, further education, and career paths. It is truly a book that every student above the middle school level should read. Because the schools in various cities have just started, the book is popular throughout the country and selling extremely well. The price is two yuan per copy, but for the benefit of readers, it is being offered at a special price of one yuan and twenty cents, plus sixteen cents for postage. The store at 554 Fourth Malu also sells the book at the same price.

Suzhou Xuejiawan Village Elementary School Seeks Teachers 225

In memory of their ancestor, Mr. You Sui, the You brothers of Suzhou have specially donated 240 mu of inherited fields as a school fund. They will first establish a village elementary school in Xuejiawan Village, Wuxian County. Their ambition is threefold: first, to cultivate the children of village farmers, hoping to develop agricultural and industrial talents with scientific knowledge and skills to meet the needs of modern agriculture and industry; second, to materially improve the living conditions of the farmers in the village within a reasonable period; and third, to alleviate the suffering of farmers and increase their productivity to the best of their ability economically using appropriate methods. The qualifications for teachers are as follows: 1. Healthy physique; 2. Age between 20 and 25; 3. Strong desire to serve in village education; 4. Ability to speak the dialect of the Suzhou-Shanghai area; 5. At least a high school education or equivalent; 6. Possessing a desire to help others and rich general knowledge; 7. A married couple willing to work together. Compensation: Monthly salary of 30 yuan, 5 yuan for the wife's meal allowance. Housing includes one bedroom, one living room, one kitchen, and one bathroom/toilet in addition to the classroom. All equipment is complete, and the school possesses a radio, a daily newspaper, books, and magazines, etc. Those who believe they are qualified should submit a resume and a handwritten letter to the following addresses. Suitable candidates will be contacted for an interview. Unsuitable candidates will not receive a response. Personal visits will not be accepted. Addresses: You Huaixi, Free Farm, No. 260 Yanping Road, Shanghai; You Qitao, Free Farm, No. 22 Liujiawan, Suzhou.

Jiangsu Education Department Improves and Develops Village Education 226

(Zhenjiang Dispatch) The Jiangsu Education Department will be implementing the local education facilities for this year as ordered, and will pay attention to the development of village education. The report has been submitted to the Ministry of Education, and the ministry has now approved it for record. The main points of the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department's improvement and development of village education facilities are listed below:

(1) Establishing Village Education Research Associations and Training Courses: Village Education Research Associations will be established in various rural areas, bringing together people engaged in rural education in the area to study practical issues related to village education and encourage them to strive for further study. Teachers who do not meet the qualifications will attend training courses during the winter and summer vacations to enhance their knowledge and skills.

(2) Improving the Salaries of Rural Education Personnel: The salaries of rural education personnel have always been lower than those in urban areas, which affects the effectiveness of the work. Starting this year, the goal is to ensure that the salaries of teachers in urban and rural areas are equal.

(3) Improving Rural School Equipment: Rural school equipment is often simple and crude. Starting this year, funds will be actively increased to improve rural school equipment, and standards for rural school equipment will be established and ordered to be followed.

(4) Expanding Village Education: Starting this year, when local education funds increase, 80% of the total amount will be used for village education. Cooperative schools and cooperative classes will be actively added in various rural areas to ensure that all school-age children have the opportunity to attend school. Farmers' Education Centers will be added in various rural areas to continuously improve the knowledge of farmers, who account for more than 80% of China's population, and to enrich rural production. Each rural school and Farmers' Education Center must be attached to a public school to supplement the school's teaching. Appendix for the 22nd year.
